අන්තර්ගත ප්‍රධාන කරුණු

ප්‍රතිඥාව:

ගරු කරුණාරත්න පරණචිතානගේ මහතා [තීරුව 579]
ජනාධිපතිතුමාගෙන්‌ ලත්‌ සන්දේශය:

මහජන ආරක්ෂක ප්‍රකාශනය [තීරුව 579]

නිවේදන:
පාර්ලිමේන්තු මන්ත්‍රී ගරු තලතා අතුකොරල මහත්මියගේ
ඉල්ලා අස්වීම [තීරුව 580]

මාර්ගගත ක්‍රමචල සුරක්ෂිත භාවය පිළිබඳ (සංශෝධන) පනත්‌
කෙටුම්පත: ශ්‍රේෂ්ඨාධිකරණයට පෙනතසම්‌ [තීරුව 581]

ශ්‍රී ලංකා මහ බැංකුවේ කර්තව්‍යය සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌
පාර්ලිමේන්තුව දැනුවත්‌ කිරීම සඳහා වන විශේෂ රැස්වීම

[තීරුව 582]
විගණකාධිපතිවරයාගේ වාර්තාව [තීරුව 583]
රජයේ මුදල්‌ පිළිබඳ කාරක සභාවේ වාර්තාව [තීරුව 591]
ආංශික අධීක්ෂණ කාරක සභා වාර්තා [තීරුව 592]

ප්‍රශ්නවලට වාචික පිළිතුරු [තීරු 598-649]
පෞද්ගලිකව දැනුම්‌ දීමෙන්‌ ඇසූ ප්‍රශ්නය:
11/11/ චැඩසටහනෙහි බලපෑම [තීරුව 660]

ශ්‍රී ලංකාවේ සත්‍යය, සමගිය සහ ප්‍රතිසන්ධානය wens Om
කොමිෂන්‌ සභාව පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පත:
පළමුවන චර කියවන ලදී [තීරුව 665]

ජාතික ඉඩම්‌ කොමිෂන්‌ සභාව පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පත:
පළමුවන චර කියවන ලදී [නීරුව 606]

සමාගම්‌ (සංශෝධන) පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පත:
පළමුවන චර කියවන ලදී [නීරුව 607]

විදේශ නඩු තීන්දු අනෝ‍යාන්‍යව පිළිගැනීම, ලියාපදිංචි කිරීම සහ
බලාත්මක කිරීම පිළිබඳ පනන්‌ කෙටුම්පත :
දෙවන චර සහ තුන්වන චර කියවා සංශෝධිතාකාරයෙන්‌
සම්මත කරන ලදී [නීරු 069-751 ]
අපරාධ නඩු විධාන සංග්‍රහය (සංශෝධන) පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පත :
දෙවන වර සහ තුන්චන චර කියවා සංශෞධිතාකාරයෙන්‌
සම්මත කරන ලදී [නීරු 751-754]
සේවකයන්ගේ ජාතික අවම චේතනය (සංශෝධන) පනත්‌

කෙටුම්පත:

දෙවන චර සහ තුන්වන චර කියවා සම්මන කරන ලදී
[නීරු 754-756]

 

பிரதான உள்ளடக்கம்‌

உறுதிப்பிரமாணம்‌:
மாண்புமிகு கருணாரத்ன பரணவிதானகே [ப:579]

சனாதிபதியிடமிருந்து வந்த செய்தி:
பொதுசனப்‌ பாதுகாப்புப்‌ பிரகடனம்‌ [ப: 579]

அறிவிப்புகள்‌:
பாராளுமன்ற உறுப்பினர்‌ மாண்புமிகு (திருமதி) தலதா
அத்துகோரலவினது இராஜினாமா [ப: 580]

நிகழ்நிலைக்‌ காப்பு (திருத்தம்‌) சட்டமூலம்‌:
உயர்நீதிமன்றுக்கு மனுக்கள்‌ [ப: 581]

இலங்கை மத்திய வங்கியின்‌ கடமைகள்‌ தொடர்பில்‌
பாராளுமன்றுக்கு விளக்கமளிக்கும்‌ விசேட

கூட்டம்‌ [ப: 582]
கணக்காய்வாளர்‌ அதிபதியினது அறிக்கை [ப: 583]
அரசாங்க நிதி பற்றிய குழுவின்‌ அறிக்கை [ப: 591]
துறைசார்‌ மேற்பார்வைக்‌ குழு அறிக்கைகள்‌ [ப: 592]
வினாக்களுக்கு வாய்மூல விடைகள்‌ [ப: 598 - 649]

தனி அறிவித்தல்‌ மூல வினா:
111 நிகழ்ச்சித்‌ திட்டத்தின்‌ தாக்கம்‌ [ப: 660]

இலங்கையில்‌ உண்மை, ஒற்றுமை
நல்லிணக்கத்துக்கான ஆணைக்குழு சட்டமூலம்‌:
முதன்முறை மதிப்பிடப்பட்டது [ப: 665]

மற்றும்‌

தேசிய காணி ஆணைக்குழு சட்டமூலம்‌:
முதன்முறை மதிப்பிடப்பட்டது [ப: 666]
கம்பெனிகள்‌ (திருத்தம்‌) சட்டமூலம்‌:
முதன்முறை மதிப்பிடப்பட்டது [ப: 667]
வெளிநாட்டு தீர்ப்புக்களைப்‌ பரஸ்பரம்‌ ஏற்றங்கீகரித்தல்‌,
பதிவுசெய்தல்‌ மற்றும்‌ வலுவுறுத்தல்‌ சட்டமூலம்‌:
இரண்டாம்‌, மூன்றாம்‌ முறைகள்‌ மதிப்பிடப்பட்டு
திருத்தப்பட்டவாறு நிறைவேற்றப்பட்டது
[ப: 669-751]

குற்றவியல்‌ நடவடிக்கைமுறைச்‌ சட்டக்கோவை (திருத்தம்‌)

சட்டமூலம்‌:

இரண்டாம்‌, மூன்றாம்‌ முறைகள்‌ மதிப்பிடப்பட்டு
திருத்தப்பட்டவாறு நிறைவேற்றப்பட்டது
[ப: 751-754]

வேலையாளர்களின்‌ தேசிய குறைந்தபட்ச வேதனம்‌
(திருத்தம்‌) சட்டமூலம்‌:

இரண்டாம்‌, மூன்றாம்‌ முறைகள்‌ மதிப்பிடப்பட்டு

நிறைவேற்றப்பட்டது [ப:754-756]

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, මට පැහැදිලි කිරීමක්‌ කරන්න

ගරු කථානායකතුමා

(மாண்புமிகு சபாநாயகர்‌ அவர்கள்‌)

(The Hon. Speaker)

ඔව්‌, ගරු විපක්ෂයේ ප්‍රධාන සංවිධායකතුමා.

ගරු නීතිඥ ලක්ෂ්මන්‌ කිරිඇල්ල මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு சட்டத்தரணி லக்ஷ்மன்‌ கிரிஎல்ல)

(The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella, Attorney-at-Law)

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, පසුගිය අවුරුදු හතරහමාර තුළ මහ
බැංකුවේ අධිපතිතුමා පාර්ලිමේන්තුවට ඇවිල්ලා ඔය කියන
විධියට පැහැදිලී කිරීමක්‌ කෙරුවේ නැහැ නේ. දැන්‌ මේ කරන්නේ,
අශ්චයා පැනලා ගියාට පස්සේ ඉස්තාලය වහනවා වාගේ වැඩක්‌.
විශේෂයෙන්ම අරගළය පැවැති කාලයේ මහ බැංකුවේ මුදල්‌ නැහැ
කියලා, පාර්ලිමේන්තුවට ඇවිල්ලා පැහැදිලී කිරීමක්‌ කරන්න
එතුමාට වගකීමක්‌ තිබුණා. නමුත්‌, එතුමා එහෙම කළේ.' නැහැ.
පසුව පාර්ලිමේන්තු මන්ත්‍රීවරුන්‌ එතුමාගෙන්‌ ඉල්ලීමක්‌ කළාට
පසුවයි එහෙම කළේ. ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, ඔබතුමාත්‌ ඒ
අවස්ථාවට සහභාගි වුණා. එදා තමයි ඒ සියල්ල හෙළි වුණේ. මට

593 පාර්ලිමේන්තුව 594

[ගරු මයන්ත දිසානායක මහතා]

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, ඒ එක්කම මේ අවස්ථාව ප්‍රයෝජනයට
ගන්න මා කැමැතියි, අපේ සියලුම සාමාජික මන්ත්‍රීවරුන්ටත්‌, ඒ
වාගේම අනුකමිටුවේ සභාපති ගරු වෛද්‍ය උපුල්‌ ගලප්පත්ති
මැතිතුමාටත්‌, සියලුම සාමාජිකයන්ටත්‌, අපේ ආංශික අධීක්ෂණ
කාරක සභාවේ ලේකම්චරිය චන නිරංජලා ලක්ෂානි මැතිනිය
ඇතුළු සියලුම නිලධාරීින්ටත්‌, අපේ අමාත්‍යාංශයේ සුනිල්‌ ද
අල්විස්‌ මැතිතුමා, රශ්නි හෙට්ටිගේ මැතිනිය ඇතුළු අනෙකුත්‌
නිලධාරීන්ටත්‌ ස්තුති කරන්න.

ගරු නීතිඥ උදයන කිරිඳිගොඩ මහතං

(மாண்புமிகு சட்டத்தரணி உதயன கிரிந்திகொட)

(The Hon. Udayana Kirindigoda, Attorney-at-Law)

ගරු කථානායකතුම්නි, විවෘත සහ වගකීවයුතු රජයක්‌ පිළිබඳ
ආංශික අධීක්ෂණ කාරක සභාවේ සභාපතිතුමා වෙනුවෙන්‌ මම්‌
එම්‌ කාරක සභාව වෙන යොමු කරන ලද ~

1 2022 වර්ෂය සඳහා මානව සම්පත්‌ සංවර්ධනය කීරීමේ
ඳූ
ලංකා ජාතික සභාවේ චාර්ෂික චාර්තාව; සහ

(ii) 2020 සහ 2021 වර්ෂ සඳහා අධිකරණ සේවා කොමිෂන්‌
සභා ලේකම්‌ කාර්යාලයේ චාර්ෂික කාර්ය සාධන චාර්තා

සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌ එකී කාරක සභාවේ චාර්තාව ඉදිරිපත්‌ කරමි.

மரம ඔන නම්ය ය්‍රශයය Rouslo mow eé.
சுபரா த்தில்‌ இருக்கச்‌ கட்டனையிடப்பட்டது.

(மாண்புமிகு சட்டத்தரணி உதயன கிரிந்திகொட)

ආංශික අධීක්ෂණ කාරක සභාවේ සභාපතිතුමා වෙනුවෙන්‌ මම්‌

(1) 2022 වර්ෂය සඳුහා ජාතික පොලිස්‌ කොමිෂන්‌ සභාවේ

(1) 2022 වර්ෂය සඳහා ඉඩම්‌ පරිභරණ ප්‍රතිපත්ති සැලයුම්‌

ගරු (වෛදා) කචින්ද හේෂාන්‌ ජයවර්ධන මහතා
(வைத்திய கலாநிதி)
ஜயவர்தன)

(The Hon. (Dr.) Kavinda Heshan Jayawardhana)
ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, මගේ පළමුවැනි අතුරු ප්‍රශ්නය මෙයයි.

(மாண்புமிகு கவிந்த ஹேஷான்‌

ගරු ඇමතිතුමනි, අපි එදා විශේෂයෙන්‌ හම්බන්නොට චරාය
චීන සමාගමකට ලබා දුන්නා. මට මනක විධියට එයින්‌
ඇමෙරිකානු ඩොලර්‌ බිලියන 1.2කට ආසන්න මුදල්‌ ප්‍රමාණයක්‌
අපේ රජයට ලැබුණා. එතැනින්‌ පසුව ශ්‍රී ලංකා රජයට චීන-
හම්බන්තොට වරායෙන්‌ යම්කිසි ආදායමක්‌ ලැබෙනවාද කියලා
ම්ම දැන ගන්න කැමැතියි.

ගරු නීතිඥ නිමල්‌ සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு சட்டத்தரணி நிமல்‌ சிறிபால த சில்வா)

(The Hon. Nimal Siripala de Silva, Attorney-at-Law)

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, එතුමාගේ මුල්‌ ප්‍රශ්නය තුළ ඔය
ප්‍රශ්නය අහලා නැහැ. ඒක අහලා තිබුණා නම්‌ අවශ්‍ය තොරතුරු
ලබාගෙන ඒ පිළිබඳව දන්වන්න මට පුළුවන්කම තිබුණා. ගරු
මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි, ඉදිරියේදී ඔබතුමා එය වෙනත්‌ ප්‍රශ්නයක්‌ හැටියට

අදාළ නොවේ.

ගරු ඉම්රාන්‌ මහරූෆ්‌ මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு இம்ரான்‌ மஹ்ரூப்‌)

(The Hon. Imran Maharoof)

நன்றி, கெனரவ சபாநாயகர்‌ இந்தக்‌
கேள்வியானது, பல வருடங்களுக்கு முன்னர்‌ என்னால்‌ சமர்ப்‌
பிக்கப்பட்டதாகும்‌. இன்று இதற்குப்‌ பதில்‌ அளித்தமைக்கு
கெளரவ அமைச்சர்‌ அவர்களுக்கு நன்றி கூறுகின்றேன்‌.

அவர்களே!

கெளரவ அமைச்சர்‌ அவர்களே, இன்று விவசாயிகள்‌
மிகவும்‌ கஷ்டத்துக்கு மத்தியிலேயே தங்களுடைய விவசாயச்‌
செயற்பாடுகளை முன்னெடுத்து வருகின்றார்கள்‌. எனினும்‌,
அ நெல்லுக்கு நிர்ணய விலை இல்லாத
காரணத்தால்‌ அவர்கள்‌ பல வழிகளிலும்‌ பாதிக்கப்‌
பட்டுக்கொண்டு இருக்கின்றார்கள்‌. எனவே, உங்களுடைய
அமைச்சின்‌ மூலமாக நெல்லுக்கான நிர்ணய விலையைத்‌
தீர்மானிப்பதற்குரிய ஏதாவதொரு வேலைத்திட்டம்‌
முன்னெடுக்கப்படுகின்றதா? எனக்‌ கேட்கின்றேன்‌. குறிப்பாக,

வர்களுடைய

 

நெல்‌ உற்பத்தி கூடுதலாக மேற்கொள்ளப்படுகின்ற மாவட்டங்‌

களிலாவது உடனடியாக அமுல்படுத்தக்கூடிய வகையில்‌
ஏதாவது ஒரு வேலைத்திட்டம்‌ உங்களுடைய அமைச்சிடம்‌
இருக்கின்றதா? என்பதுதான்‌ என்னுடைய முதலாவது

மேலதிகக்‌ கேள்வியாகும்‌.

ගරු මහින්ද අමරවීර මහතං

(மாண்புமிகு மஹிந்த அமரவீர)

(The Hon. Mahinda Amaraweera)

ගරු කථානායකතුම්නි, වී මිලදී ගැනීම සඳහා දැන්‌ අපට මූල්‍ය
ප්‍රතිපාදන ලැබී තිබෙනවා. අපි වී ගබඩා චිවෘත කර තිබෙනවා. ඒ
අනුව, දැනටමත්‌ කීරි සම්බා විශාල ප්‍රමාණයක්‌ අපට ලැබී
තිබෙනවා. අඛණ්ඩව වී මිලදී ගැනීම අපි සිදු කරනවා. නමුත්‌, අද
තිබෙන තත්ත්වය තම්යි, රජයේ මිලට වඩා ඉහළ මිලකට
පෞද්ගලික අංශය වී මිලදී ගැනීම. ගොචීන්ට හොඳ සාධාරණ
මිලක්‌ ලැබීම පිළිබඳව අපි සතුටු චනචා. චීචලට ස්ථාවර මිලක්‌
නියම කර තිබෙනවා. ගොඩක්‌ කට්ටිය විශේෂයෙන්ම ජනතා
චීමුක්ති පෙරමුණ නිරන්තරයෙන්ම ගොවියාට චී මීල සම්බන්ධ
ගණන්‌ කියනවා. මම හීතන විධියට ඒ කිසිම කණ්ඩායමක්‌ වී
මිලයි, හාල්‌ මිලයි හරියට ගළපලා කථා කරන්නේ නැහැ. ම්ම
දඇක්කා, නාඩු චී කීලොචවක්‌ රුපියල්‌ 150කට මිලදී ගන්න ඕනෑය
කියලා එතුමන්ලාගේ ගොවි සංවිධාන එකමුතුව ද මොකක්ද
කියන එකකින්‌ ප්‍රකාශයක්‌ කළා. වී කිලෝචක්‌ රුපියල්‌ 150ට
මිලදී ගන්නවා නම්‌ හාල්‌ කීලොවක්‌ රුපියල්‌ 3000ක්‌ වෙනවා. ඒ
නිසා මම්‌ කියන්නේ, කචුරුන්‌ හෝ වී මිලදී ගැනීම ගැන කථා
කරනවා නම්‌, ගොචියා ගැන කථා කරනචා නම්‌, චී මිල ගැනත්‌
කථා කරන්න, ඒ වාගේම්‌ පාරිභෝගිකයන්ට භාල්‌ ලබා දෙන මිල
ගැනත්‌ කථා කරන්න කියලායි. මේක මම හැම දාම කියනවා.
නිකම්‌ බොරුවට ගොවීන්ගේ පැත්තට ගිගිල්ලා චී මිල ගැන කථා
කරන්නත්‌, පාරිභෝගිකයාගේ පැත්තට ආචාම අඩුවට හාල්‌ දෙන
එක ගැන කථා කරන්නන්‌ නොවෙයි, හරියට කෙළින්‌ ඉඳගෙන
කථා කරන්න කියලා ඒ සියලු පාර්ශ්වයන්ගෙන්‌ මම ඉල්ලීමක්‌
කරනවා.

ඒ වාගේම මම ඔබතුමාට කියන්න කැමැතියි. පොහොර සඳහා
(ලබා දෙන සහනාධාර මුදල්‌ වැඩි කර දෙන්න අපි ~රජය- තීන්දු
කළ බව. ඒ අනුව, ලබන මාසයේ ඉඳලාම පොහොර නිකුන්‌
කරන්න කටයුතු කරනවා. ඒ සඳූහා කැබිනට්‌ අනුමැතිය ලැබී
තිබෙනවා. එතකොට රුපියල්‌ 4,000ක වාගේ මිලක්‌ තමයි
පොහොර හොණ්ඩරයක්‌ වෙනුවෙන්‌ ගෙෆාචීන්ට වැය කරන්න
වෙන්නේ. ඒ සහනය ගොවි ජනතාව චෙනුවෙන්‌ ලබා දෙන්න අපි
කටයුතු කරලා තිබෙනවා. මොකද, පොහොර සහනාධාරය සහ
අනෙකුත්‌ සහනාධාර ලබා දීම තුළින්‌ රජය බලාපොරොත්තු
වෙන්නේ මුළු රටේම පුරවැසියන්ට ඒ සහනය ලබා දෙන්නයි.
මොකද, ගොවියාට චී නිෂ්පාදනය සඳහා වැය චන මුදල අඩු
වෙනවා නම්‌ සහල්‌ අඩු මීලට ලබා දෙන්න පුළුවන්‌. ඒ වෙනුවෙන්‌
නමයි රජය මේ මූල්‍ය ප්‍රදාන ලබා දෙන්න කටයුතු කරන්නේ.

609 පාර්ලිමේන්තුව 610

ගරු ඉම්රාන්‌ මහරූෆ්‌ මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு இம்ரான்‌ மஹ்ரூப்‌)

(The Hon. Imran Maharoof)

OG MHmomMQeH, මගේ දෙවැනි අතුරු ප්‍රශ්නය මෙයයි.

நன்றி, கெளரவ அமைச்சர்‌ அவர்களே! எனது இரண்டாவது
மேலதிகக்‌ கேள்வியைக்‌ கேட்கின்றேன்‌.

எங்களுடைய திருகோணமலை மாவட்டத்திலுள்ள
விவசாயிகள்‌ எதிர்நோக்குகின்ற பாரியதொரு பிரச்சினைதான்‌,
நெல்லைக்‌ காய வைப்பதற்கான இட வசதிகள்‌ இல்லாமை.
திருகோணமலையிலுள்ள குறிப்பாக, கிண்ணியா, மூதூர்‌,
தோப்பூர்‌, தம்பலகாமம்‌, குச்சவெளி போன்ற பிரதேசங்‌
களிலுள்ள விவசாயிகளுக்குத்‌ தங்களுடைய நெல்லைக்‌ காய
வைப்பதற்கான இட வசதிகளை ஏற்படுத்திக்‌ கொடுப்பதற்கு
உங்களுடைய  அமைச்சின்மூலம்‌ ஏதாவது திட்டங்கள்‌
முன்னெடுக்கப்படுகின்றதா? எனவும்‌ அந்தப்‌ பிரதேசத்தில்‌
இருக்கின்ற விவசாயிகளுடைய நெல்லைக்‌ களஞ்சியப்‌
படுத்துவற்கான இலகுவான வழிமுறைகளைச்‌
கொடுப்பதற்கான நடவடிக்கைகள்‌ ஏதாவது உங்களுடைய

செய்து

அமைச்சின்மூலம்‌ முன்னெடுக்கப்படுகின்றதா? எனவும்‌ நான்‌
கெளரவ அமைச்சரிடம்‌ கேட்க விரும்புகின்றேன்‌.

ගරු මඟින්ද අමරවීර මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு மஹிந்த அமரவீர)

(The Hon. Mahinda Amaraweera)

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, චී වේළීම සම්බන්ධ ප්‍රශ්නයක්‌
තිබෙනවා. ඒ නිසා තමයි චී අලෙවි මණ්ඩලයට අයන්‌ සෑම්‌

asked the Prime Minister and the Minister of Public
Administration, Home Affairs, Provincial Councils and
Local Government:

(4) Will he inform this House -

(1) whether he accepts that the residents living
in rented houses face various difficulties in

Cards due to the inability of establishing the

(b) If not, why?

ගරු අශෝක ප්‍රියන්ත මහතා (ස්වදේශ කටයුතු රාජා
අමාත්‍යාතුමා)
(மாண்புமிகு அசோக்க
இராஜாங்க அமைச்சர்‌)
(The Hon. Ashoka Priyantha - State Minister of Home
Affairs)
ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, අග්‍රාමාත්‍ය සහ රාජා පරිපාලන.
ස්වදේශ කටයුතු, පළාත්‌ සභා හා පළාත්‌ පාලන අමාත්‍යතුමා
වෙනුවෙන්‌ මා එම ප්‍රශ්නයට පිළිතුරු ලබා දෙනවා.

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, ඒ වාගේම රාජා සේවයේ අත්‍යවශ්‍ය
සේවා සඳහා නිලධාරීන්ගේ අවශ්‍යතාව තිබෙනවා. ඒ අනාවශ්‍ය
සේවාවල සහ නිලධාරින්ගේ ගැටලු විසඳන්න රජයක්‌ විධියට,
අමාත්‍යාංශයක්‌ විඨියට අපි කටයුතු කර තිබෙනවා. ගරු
අගමැතිතුමාගේ උපදෙස්‌ සහ එතුමාගේ මැදිහත්‌ වීම මත අවශ්‍ය
තනතුරු පුරවන්න කටයුතු කර තිබෙනවා. අග්‍රාමාත්‍ය
ලේකම්තුමාගේ ප්‍රධානත්වයෙන්‌ කමිටුවක්‌ පත්‌ කරලා ඒ කටයුතු

ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි, බහුකාර්ය සංවර්ධන සභායකයන්‌ හැටියට
දරුවන්‌ විශාල පිරිසක්‌ බඳවාගෙන කිසිම විෂයක්‌ නැතුව නැන්‌

අසීරු- අවස්ථාවේ ඒ අයත්‌ රාජ්‍ය සේවයට ඇතුළන්‌ කරලා, රාජ්‍ය

කරලා තිබෙනවා. ඉදිරියේ දී අමුතුවෙන්‌ කරන්න දෙයක්‌ නැහැ.

සේවය ශක්තිමත්‌ කරන්න, රාජ්‍ය නිලධාරින්ට පහයුකම්‌
සපයන්න, ඔවුන්ගේ වැටුප්‌ වැඩි කරන්න දැවැන්න කාර්යභාරයක්‌
ඉෂ්ට කරලා තිබෙනවා.

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, චර්තමානයේ දී නම්‌ බොහෝ අය
ජනාධිපතිවරණය ඉලක්ක කරලා අරවා දෙනවා, මේවා දෙනවා
කියලා කියනවා.

ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමා පුළුල්ව අහන කාරණාවට මට උත්තරයක්‌
සපයන්න බැහැ. නමුන්‌ අපි අමාත්‍යාංශයක්‌ විධියට රාජ්‍ය සේවය
ශක්තිමත්‌ කරලා, ඔවුන්ට ජීවත්‌ වෙන්න පුළුවන්‌ චේතනයක්‌
නිර්මාණය කිරීමටන්‌, ඔවුන්ගේ ගෞරවය ආරක්ෂා කරන්නත්‌
කටයුතු කර තිබෙනවා. 2025 වර්ෂය සඳහා ඔවුන්ගේ වැටුප්‌ වැඩි

ගියොත්‌ ලොකු වෙලාවක්‌ යන නිසා මම ඒ ගැන කියන්නේ නැහැ.
මේ වෙද්දි ඒක ගැන මාධ්‍යයෙන්‌, එහෙන්‌, මෙහෙන්‌ දැනගන්න
පුළුවන්කම ලැබෙනවා.

ගරු ඉෂාක්‌ රහුමාන්‌ මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு இஷாக்‌ ரஹுமான்‌)

(The Hon. Ishak Rahuman)

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, මගේ දෙවැනි අතුරු ප්‍රශ්නය මෙයයි.

ගරු රාජ්‍ය ඇමතිතුමනි, මේ කාලයේ හැම්‌ වේදිකාවකම්‌
පොරොන්දු දෙනවා, රජයේ සේවකයන්ගේ පඩි වැඩි කරනවා
කියලා. ගරු අගමැතිතුමාත්‌ මේ අවස්ථාවේ සභාවේ සිටින නිසා
මම මේ කාරණය අහන්න කැමැතියි. ගරු අගමැතිතුමනී, රජයේ
සේවකයන්ට රුපියල්‌ 25,000කින්‌ පඩි වැඩි කිරීමට කැබිනට්‌
මණ්ඩල අනුමැතියක්‌ අරගෙන තිබෙනවා කියලා කියනවා. රනිල්‌
වික්‍රමසිංහ මැතිතුමා මේ ජනාධිපතිවරණය ජයග්‍රහණය කරලා
නැවතන්‌ ජනාධිපතිවරයා විධියට පත්‌ වුණොත්‌ 2025දී එම
රුපියල්‌ 25,000ක වැටුප්‌ වැඩිවීම අනිචාර්යයෙන්ම ලබා
දෙනවාද, එහෙම නැත්නම්‌ ඒක පොරොන්දුවක්‌ පමණද කියලායි
ම්ම අහන්නෙ. /ණාධ්‍ය ක්‍කිරීම/ධ

ගරු අශොක ප්‍රියන්ත මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு அசோக்க பிரியந்த)

(The Hon. Ashoka Priyantha)

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, රජයේ නිලධාරින්ට කාගෙන්‌ හරි පඩි
වැඩිවීමක්‌ වෙනවා නම්‌, ස්වදේශ කටයුතු රාජ්‍ය අමාතාචරයා
විධියට මම ගොඩක්‌ සතුටු වෙනවා. මේ තිබෙන දරිද්‍රතාව මත
ජීවත්‌ වෙන්න සුදුසු චැටුපක්‌ -චේතනයක්‌- ලැබෙනවා නම්‌, කවුරු
හරි පඩි වැඩි කරනවා නම්‌, මේ කාල සීමාව තුළ ඔවුන්ට ලබා දුන්‌
පොරොන්දු ඉටු වෙනවා නම්‌, රාජ්‍ය අමාත්‍යවරයා විධියට මම
ඉතාම සතුටු වෙනවා. හැබැයි මම ඔබතුමාටත්‌, මේ සභාවටන්‌
කිව්වා, අමාත්‍යාංශයක්‌ විධියට අපි බොරු පොරොන්දු දෙන්නේ
නැහැ කියලා. මේ වෙද්දී අපට කරන්න පුළුවන්‌ කාර්යභාරය අපි
කර තිබෙනවා. ඒ ගැන නැවත කියන්න ඕනෑ නැහැ. 2024
අචුරුද්දේන්‌ අපි රුපියල්‌ 10,000ක පඩි වැඩිවීමක්‌ කර තිබෙනවා.
2025දීත්‌ ඒ වැඩි කිරීම අපි අමාත්‍යාංශයක්‌ විධියට කරන්න
බලාපොරොත්තු වෙනවා.

ගරු කථානායකතුමා

கல்வி அமைச்சரைக்‌ கேட்ட வினா:

(அ) (0) இலங்கை அதிபர்‌ சேவையிலும்‌ இலங்கை
ஆசிரியர்‌ சேவையிலுமுள்ள அலுவலர்களுக்‌
கென திட்டவட்டமான இடமாற்றக்‌ கொள்கை
யொன்று உள்ளதா என்பதையும்‌;

(4)  ஆமெனில்‌, மேற்படி இடமாற்றக்‌ கொள்கையில்‌
உள்ளடங்கியுள்ள பிரதானமான விடயங்களும்‌
அளவுகோல்களும்‌ யாவையென்பதையும்‌ :

(1) இலங்கை கல்வி நிருவாக சேவையிலுள்ள அலு
வலர்களுக்கென திட்டவட்டமான இடமாற்றக்‌
கொள்கையொன்று நடைமுறையிலில்லை என்‌
பதை அறிவாரா என்பதையும்‌;

(iv) ஆமெனில்‌, இலங்கை கல்வி நிருவாக சேவை
யிலுள்ள அலுவலர்களுக்காக திட்டவட்டமான
இடமாற்றக்‌ கொள்கையொன்றை நடைமுறைப்‌
படுத்துவதற்கு எடுக்கப்படும்‌ நடவடிக்கைகள்‌
யாவையென்பதையும்‌;

(The Hon. (Dr.} Susil Premajayantha, Attorney-at-Law)

ගරු නීතිඥ (ආචාර්ය) සුසිල්‌ ප්‍රේමජයන්ත මහතා

(The Hon. (Dr.) Susil Premajayantha, Attorney-at-Law)

ඒ අය බඳවා ගෙන නැහැ. ඒ ගොල්ලන්‌ ඉතා හොඳ ප්‍රතිඵල ගත්ත
අය. මම අහන්නේ ඒ ගොල්ලන්‌ බඳවා ගන්න අපි කැබිනට්‌
පත්‍රිකාවක්‌ දමනවාද කියලායි.

දෙවැනි කාරණය. දැනට ගුරු පුහුණුවක්‌ ක්‍රියාත්මක කරගෙන
යනවා. ඒක හෙට අනිද්දා පටන්‌ ගන්නවා. සිවිල්‌ ආරක්ෂක
බලකායෙන්‌ පඩි දෙන ගමන්‌ ඒ ගොල්ලන්‌ ඒ ගුරු පුහුණුවට
අනුයුක්ත කරන්න අපට බැරිද? මොකද, ගැසට්‌ එකේ එහෙම
දෙයක්‌ නැති නිසා අද ඔබතුමා ඒකට අනුමැතිය දුන්නොත්‌, ඒ
අයට ඒක ලොකු දෙයක්‌ වෙනවා. එතකොට ගුරු පුහුණුවෙන්‌
පසුව ඒ ගොල්ලන්‌ අනුයුක්ත කරන්න පුළුවන්‌.

631 2024 සැප්තැම්බර්‌ 03 632

ගරු නීතිඥ (ආචාර්ය) සුසිල්‌ ප්‍රේමජයන්ත මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு சட்டத்தரணி (கலாநிதி) சுசில்‌ பிரேமஜயந்த)

(The Hon. (Dr.) Susil Premajayantha, Attorney-at-Law)

මට බලයක්‌ නැහැ පළාත්‌ පන්වීමක්‌ දෙන්න. ඒ නිසායි මා ඒ
කටයුත්ත එහෙම කළේ. මට පුළුවන්‌ නම්‌ මම මෙලහකටත්‌ ඒ
පත්වීම්‌ දීලා.

ගරු ගෙවිඳු කුමාරතුංග මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு கெவிந்து குமாரதுங்க)

(The Hon. Gevindu Cumaratunga)

මේ කාරණය අපි ගරු අගමැතිතුමාගේ අවධානයට යොමු
කරනවා.

ගරු නීතිඥ (ආචාර්ය) සුසිල්‌ ප්‍රේමජයන්ත මහතා
(மாண்புமிகு சட்டத்தரணி (கலாநிதி) சுசில்‌ பிரேமஜயந்த)
(The Hon. (Dr.) Susil Premajayantha, Attorney-at-Law)
හොඳයි.

ගරු දයාසිරි ජයසේකර මහතා
(மாண்புமிகு தயாசிறி ஜயசேகர)
(The Hon. Dayasiri Jayasekara)
මුලාසනාරූඞ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි,-

ගරු මූලාසනාරූඬ මන්ත්‍රීතුමා

(மாண்புமிகு தலைமைதாங்கும்‌ உறுப்பினர்‌ அவர்கள்‌)

(The Hon. Presiding Member)

දැන්‌ දහදෙනෙක්‌ චිතර ගරු අධ්‍යාපන ඇමතිතුමාගෙන්‌ ප්‍රශ්න

ඇහුවා.

ගරු දයාසිරි ජයසේකර මන්ත්‍රීතුමා.

ගරු දයාසිරි ජයසේකර මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு தயாசிறி ஜயசேகர)

(The Hon. Dayasiri Jayasekara)

මා ප්‍රශ්නය අහන්නේ එතුමාගෙන්‌ නොවෙයි. විදේශ කටයුතු
ඇමතිතුමා දැන්‌ මේ ගරු සභාවේ සිටින නිසා. මා එතුමාගෙන්‌
කෙටියෙන්‌ ප්‍රශ්නයක්‌ අහනවා.

ගරු ඇම්තිතුමනී, ඔබතුමා දන්නවා, යුක්රේන - රුසියා
යුද්ධයට අපේ රටිනුත්‌ විශාල පිරිසක්‌ ගිහිල්ලා සිටින බව. ගිහිල්ලා
කථා කරලා, මේ ඇතිවෙච්ච ප්‍රශ්නය විසඳා ගන්න ඔබතුමා අපට
යම්‌ අවස්ථාවක්‌ ලබා දුන්නා. හැබැයි, දැන්‌ තිබෙන ප්‍රශ්නය.
රුසියාවට ගිය අය පිළිබඳව එතැනින්‌ පස්සේ කිසිම 16ළ00401ද
එකක්‌ නැති එකයි. එහේ දැන්‌ හයසිය ගණනක්‌ ඉන්නවා. ඒ අය
සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌ කරන්නේ මොකක්ද? 17දෙනෙක්‌ මීය ගියා. දැන්‌
20දෙනෙක්‌ මිය ගියා කියලා කියනවා. ඒ අයට මොකක්ද

ඒ ගොල්ලෝ අහනවා, "ඇන්‌ මොකක්ද කරන්නේ?" කියලා. ඒ
අය සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌ තිබුණු උනන්දුව, උද්‍යෝගය රජයෙන්‌
ගිලිහිලා ද, එහෙම නැත්නම්‌ ඒ අය වෙනුවෙන්‌ කරන්නේ
මොකක්ද කියලා අහනවා.

දෙන්න විධියක්‌ නැහැ. මොකද, ඒ අය දැන්‌ මේ රථින්‌ පිටට

அமைச்சரைக்‌ கேட்ட வினா:

(அ) () இலங்கைக்கு வழங்கப்பட்டுள்ள 86 Plus
நிவாரண அடிப்படையில்‌, தொழிலாளர்களின்‌
உரிமைகள்‌ மற்றும்‌ பாதுகாப்புத்‌ தொடர்பான
பல்வேறு ஏற்பாடுகளை அமுல்படுத்துமாறு
இலங்கை தேவைப்படுத்தப்பட்டுள்ளது என்பதை

அவர்‌ அறிவாரா என்பதையும்‌;

(1) அப்படியாயின்‌, தொழிலாளர்களின்‌

உரிமைகளை மேம்படுத்துவதற்கு எடுக்கப்பட்ட

நடவடிக்கைகள்‌ யாவை என்பதையும்‌;

 

(1) அவ்வாறான நடவடிக்கைகள்‌ இதுவரை
எடுக்கப்படவில்லை எனின்‌, அதற்கான
காரணங்களையும்‌;

அவர்‌ இச்சபைக்கு அறிவிப்பாரா?

(ஆ) () ஆடைத்‌ தொழிலாளர்களுக்குப்‌ பாதுகாப்பு

அறிவாரா என்பதையும்‌;

1) ஆடைத்‌ தொழிற்சாலைகளில்‌ சங்கம்‌

Sir, | am raising a point of Order with regard to the
agenda for today’s Proceedings under Standing Order
No. 22. There was a Private Members' Bill that | moved,
which was read the First time. Then, there was a petition
to the Supreme Court. The Supreme Court gave its
Determination. The Bill came up for its Second Reading
after several months, after the relevant Ministry did not
give its report within the stipulated six months. At the
Second Reading, it was passed without a debate and
a vote. Thereafter, according to the Standing Orders
under "Committee Stage of Bills" - Standing Order 57
and 58 - it was referred to the Legislative Standing
Committee chaired by the Chairman of Committees, the
Hon. Deputy Speaker himself. So, the Report of the
Legislative Standing Committee was presented to
Parliament by yourself, Hon. Deputy Speaker, on the 21"
of August, 2024.

Then, Standing Order No. 72(1) states, 1 quote:

“When a Bill has been reported to Parliament by the
Legislative Standing Committee or a Select Committee without
amendments, ...."

But, this Bill was reported with Amendments.

.. it may upon the day appointed for its consideration, be
forthwith read a third time and passed or if Parliament so direct, the
Third Reading may be postponed."

The Committee on Parliamentary Business made a
decision that the Report of the Legislative Standing
Committee would be reported to Parliament on the 21* of
August, 2024 and the Bill would be taken up for Third
Reading, in accordance with Standing Order Nos. 71, 72
and 73, today; that is, the 03" of September. The Minutes
came up before the Committee on Parliamentary
Business yesterday and was also approved. But, it is not
on the Order of Business for today, 1 understand. Why is
that? Why has it not been taken up? Yesterday, at the
Committee on Parliamentary Business, the Leader of the
House said that for certain political considerations it was
being delayed. Standing Orders do not permit delay for
political considerations. The particular Standing Order
states “...be forthwith read a third time...” The political
consideration that he has referred to is that the Illankai
Tamil Arasu Kadchi has taken a decision to support
somebody other than President Ranil Wickremesinghe.
So, this is a most horrendous thing that is happening.
Standing Orders are being violated; decisions taken at the
Committee on Parliamentary Business are being violated.

The passing of this Bill, everybody said, should be done
with consensus and its Second Reading happened without
even calling for a debate or a vote. And now, only
because our party has decided not to support the
President, it is being sabotaged, Standing Orders are
being violated.

ගරු නියොජා කථානායකතුමා
(மாண்புமிகு பிரதிச்‌ சபாநாயகர்‌ அவர்கள்‌)

657 පාර්ලිමේන්තුව 658

ගරු ඩලස්‌ අලහප්පෙරුම මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு டலஸ்‌ அழஹப்பெரும)

(The Hon. Dullas Alahapperuma)

ගරු නියෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුම්නි, මේ රටේ මහජන නියොජිත
ආයතන තුනක්‌ තිබෙනවා. අපි මේ කථා කරන වෙලාවේ ඒ
මහජන නියෝජිත ආයතන තුනෙන්‌ දෙකක්‌ වහලා තිබෙන්නේ.
ගරු සුමන්තිරන්‌ මන්ත්‍රීතුමා ඉතාම පැහැදිලිව සඳහන්‌ කළා, මෙහි
තිබෙන තාක්ෂණික කාරණා පිළිබඳව. දැන්‌ මහජන නියෝජිත
ආයතන තුනෙන්‌ දෙකක්‌ චසා තිබෙනවා. එය එක කාරණාවක්‌,
ගරු නියෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුම්නි.

දෙවැනි කාරණය හැටියට ඉතා පැහැදිලිව කිව්වා. ඒකට

ප්‍රතිපාදන නවත්වනවා. ඉතිහාසයේ ඉඳලා - 1972 ඉඳලා -

(The Hon. Dullas Alahapperuma)

ගරු නියොෝජා කථානායකතුමා

(The Hon. Deputy Speaker)

5110151016 (00111 එකට ගියාම, තව අවුරුදු ගාණක්‌ යනවා. ඒ නිසා
1998, 1999, 2000, 2001 කරපු චැරදිවලට සමහර වෙලාවට දැන්‌
තමයි දඬුවම්‌ දෙන්නෙ. නීතිය පිළිබඳ විශ්වාසය සමිපූර්ණයෙන්ම

නෛතික රාමුවක්‌ හඳුන්වා දීමයි. මේ සංශෝධනය අනුව නඩු
විභාගයට පෙනී සිටීම වෙනුවට වරද පිළිගැනීමේ එකඟතාවක්‌

හෝ වන්දි මුදල්‌ සඳහා නිර්දේශයක්‌ ලබා ගත හැක. මේ යෝජනා,
සංශෝධන මඟින්‌ අපරාධ නඩු ඵලදායී ලෙස විසඳා ගැනීමට හා
වරද පිළිගැනීමේ එකභතාව අනුව අවම දඬුවම්‌ ලබා ගැනීම තුළින්‌
බන්ධනාගාර තදබදයද අඩු කර ගැනීමට හැකියාව ඇත.

Hon. Deputy Speaker, plea agreements have proven to
be the most effective way to resolve criminal cases
worldwide. In addition, lower sentences tied to a plea
agreement address prison overcrowding. Plea agreements
are important in Sri Lanka, as there is a large backlog of
cases, which results in High Court litigation lasting up to
10 to 12 years. The backlog will continue to mount unless
some relief is provided. A plea agreement system would
expect to provide that relief.

By the proposed Amendment, the accused person and
the prosecution enter into an agreement, where the
accused would plead guilty instead of going to trial, in
consequence of which there may be reduced charges and
recommendation for a lower sentence, fine or restitution
amount. By the proposed Amendment, it is also expected
to resolve the criminal cases in an effective manner,
where lower sentences tied to plea agreement would also
address prison overcrowding.

Sir, this is a matter that the Subcommittee on Criminal
Law Reforms had been discussing for a long period of
time. Only the cases which really need to go to trial
should go to trial. Otherwise, it is a waste of time of the
lawyers, a waste of energy of everyone involved in the
process and at the end of the Day, everyone gets
exhausted. Therefore, it is accepted worldwide that a plea
agreement and a plea bargaining entered into at the
beginning between the accused and the prosecutor, which
would also be supported by the prosecutor, and presented
to court would help resolve this situation. The court
would look into that and the discretion to agree to the plea
bargain is totally vested in the court. So, we have put so
many safeguards in place in this law because in terms of
our law, everyone is presumed innocent until and unless
proven guilty. We understand that and have placed certain

safeguards in this law to protect the rights of the accused
also. However, if the accused, at one point in time, wants
to plead guilty because he knows whether he has
committed the crime or not and shorten his term, he
should also be given some sort of an inducement or
encouragement to do so without wasting time of the court
and the prosecutor and public money so that more
important matters could be taken up by the court. That is
an accepted system and | think it will open up a new
chapter in the Sri Lankan criminal justice system. I hope
that would work well and address prison overcrowding
and clear the backlog of cases in courts. So, that is the
reason behind bring in this Code of Criminal Procedure
(Amendment) Bill.

Il must also say that we are proposing two
Amendments to this Bill at the Committee Stage as there
were some concerns expressed by the Sectoral Oversight
Committee as well as by some lawyers that if you leave
the whole thing without any indication to the judge, since
the judge is not bound by the agreement entered into or
the suggestion made both by the accused and the
prosecutor, and if the judge disregards the whole thing
and gives a higher sentence, the accused could be
prejudiced.

Therefore, an Amendment has been proposed to say
“(b) Notwithstanding the recommendation of the parties,
the court shall retain the sole discretion in sentencing
and discretion to indicate the sentence that may be
imposed.” So, before reaching a final decision, if the
learned judge could indicate, “This is what 1 have in
mind”, the accused can either decide to go ahead with it
or withdraw from that and fight his case. | think that is
reasonable. | agree with that and considered it in all
aspects. 1 spoke to the Attorney-General's Department
and others and different views were expressed, but
ultimately, | thought that in a criminal justice system, the
right of an accused is very cardinal. If the accused is
going to give up his right to defend himself expecting a
reduction in his sentence, but if a routine judge gives a
higher sentence, it could be damaging and also have a
repercussion on the success of this entire law. Therefore,
we have decided to introduce that Amendment during the
Committee Stage.

So, based on the views of several experts in the field
concerned, a draft Bill was developed by the Department
of Legal Draftsman and the draft Bill consists of several
salient features. They are, one, providing provision for the
recognition and registration of a judgment for the
dissolution or annulment of a marriage or separation of
parties to a marriage, only if such judgment is obtained in
respect of a marriage registered under the Marriage
Registration Ordinance. Two, providing ground to raise
objection for recognition of a foreign judgment for the
dissolution or annulment of marriage or separation. Three,
specification of judgment to which the new law applies
and specification of the procedure to be followed by a
court of law in recognition and registering a judgment
identified by the proposed law. So, this law had
amalgamated both the laws on matrimonial judgments as
well as on money decrease. The amalgamation of both
those into one law and some of the restrictions that are
there, [ believe, are a progressive step and are better than
what is there.

But, | also feel that there are so many other areas we
could have included in this. However, since everything
has already been done now and this is a progressive
legislation than what is in existence, we will go ahead
with it and in the meantime, we need to continue to revisit
this legislation because with the inclusion of some other
areas, | feel, it could be bettered. | also feel that having
two different laws would have been ideal, one, as the
matrimonial law and the other, as the law on money
decrease because the provisions are different to each
other. However, this legislation is good; it is a long-felt
need. So many people of Sri Lankan origin who marry
here, go and live in some other countries, when they have
their matrimonial disputes, go to the courts in their
respective countries and get themselves divorced or
separated. However, when they come to Sri Lanka to get
those divorces effected or deal with the consequences of
those divorces such as getting child custody or taking
over property, there has been no proper procedure as to
how it should be done. So, this legislation will address
those issues and will, of course, serve those who are in
need of this law. If they had divorced in some other
country, they can come to Sri Lanka, register the
judgment and have it considered as a judgment of our
court, of course, subject to the rules, regulations and the
conditions in this law. Therefore, I feel this will help a
large segment, particularly the Sri Lankan expatriate
community and those who have been living outside Sri
Lanka and who wants to come back to Sri Lanka. This is
a harmless law and will only help resolve the current
situation.

So, these two legislations will help us. The one
relating to the criminal justice system will help us reduce
the backlog of court cases and speed up resolving the
issues. The other one is, of course, on the recognition and
enforcement of foreign judgments. You all know that if
there is a foreign judgment, it cannot be implemented
here unless a court in Sri Lanka empowers that.

You have to register that and get it enforced.
Enforcement of the judgment means, if you want to go
and seize a property or a bank account or even give a
minor child’s custody to the other party, a court order is
required. So, that is how this is going to help those
people. This is a long-felt need. | identified this in the
year 2000 and immediately appointed two
Subcommittees to go into those two areas.

Hopefully, we will follow this up with other relevant
laws, particularly the law relating to breakdown of the
marriage principle because in Sri Lanka, we have
stringent divorce laws, in terms of which you have to
prove a matrimonial fault. Even if the two parties have
not been living together for a long period of time, it is
almost impossible to go to court and get a divorce by
consent or by agreement because the Sri Lankan law
states that your fault has to fall within one of those three
grounds, that is, permanent impotence at the time of
marriage, adultery or malicious desertion. More or less,
80 per cent of the divorce cases today do not fall into any
of those grounds. It is just that the partners have fallen
apart and do not want to live with each other. Therefore,
because the law is such, people are being forced to and
encouraged to go to court and lie or asked to give
evidence that is not true in order to get the divorce. So, it
is time for us to move away from that and come up with
the law on breakdown of the marriage principle. That
means, if over a period, for a year or two, you have not
lived with each other and both concede that, then you
could get the divorce. That is how the Sri Lankan law had
been for a long period of time; the Sinhala law had been
so. It is under the English law that we have introduced the
marriage principle. Now, the countries which introduced
those laws, including the UK, the Netherlands and all the
other countries have moved away from those laws. We
are the only people holding onto those. So, this is a good
time for us to do that and we are in the final phase of
presenting that legislation. 1 think once you introduce
that, the duration of 80 per cent of the current divorce
cases filed on the breakdown of the marriage principle,
which, sometimes, would take such a long period of time
to contest, could be cut short.

So, we will continue to introduce such laws. I think
there are a number of laws in the pipeline, which are a
culmination of the work we started in the latter part of
2020, as 1 took over as the Minister of Justice. We
managed to revisit about 88 laws. There were about 29
Subcommittees that we had appointed. All that was
possible because the members of the legal profession
volunteered to take ownership of that work because they
thought, "All this is part of our own law, it is for our own
country and we must contribute to that". So, | am very
thankful to all those who helped us in drafting these laws,
particularly the Attorney-General’s Department for

677 පාර්ලිමේන්නුව 678

[ගරු ජනාධිපති නීතිඥ එම්‌.යූ.එම්‌. අලි සබ්රි මහතා]

incorporating those amendments and looking into the
Bills at their different stages and also the Legal
Draftsman’s Department for cooperating with us in
incorporate those amendments. We know that when you
draft a law, it goes up and down and that it is not an easy
task. Therefore, | thought it fit to mention them here and
thank them: the Subcommittee members, the Ministry
Officials, the Legal Draftsman, the Attorney-General, and
all those who got involved in drafting these laws and
submitting them for the betterment of our country.

One other important thing is, as I said earlier when the
Commission for Truth, Unity and Reconciliation in Sri
Lanka Bill was presented, we cannot be prisoners of the
past forever; we cannot live in the past and find fault with
each other. If you carefully look at the First and the
Second World Wars, those were fought among the
members of Europe. They were killing each other,
fighting with each other and ultimately, they dragged the
whole world into those. But, ultimately, after the Second
World War, after about 10, 15 years, they realized that it
is such a useless exercise to fight with each other and
thought, "If we get together, what would be the
possibilities?”

Then, the Schuman Plan was brought in. Schuman
was a former French Foreign Minister. He brought that in
the early 50s in order to create the European Union.
Today, they work together as the European Union, as a
result of which we all could see what Europe has
managed to achieve in terms of the Human Development
Index, money and everything. It is one of the wealthiest
continents in the world. Most of the people in Sri Lanka
want to go there, if they have the opportunity. Therefore,
it is important that we are not guided by the past and do
not become prisoners of the past. We must have a fresh
look at what we ought to achieve here. If those different
countries in Europe with different denominations and
different people could come together and create the
European Union, which now has their own laws in most
areas, their own customs union, their own currency and
trade facility, why cannot we not have that in this country
because we are members of the same country? And we
have a Constitution which ensures equality and also
protects the unitary status of the nation. Therefore, subject
to those limitations, we should not always use race,
religion or division for our political advancement. If you
cannot be in politics for any longer and there is no good
reason for you to be there because people are getting
united, you should leave politics rather than creating
differences among the people. Therefore, it is important,
while we respect each other, to create a country where all
of us, irrespective of our race, religion and language could
live in peace and with dignity. That would not come by
just by holding on to something which happened 50, 200
or 300 years ago. Everyone had made mistakes, but we
must move on. That moving on could be made with
determination, hard work, by giving in, sharing and
caring. | think that is how countries have developed. We
only say that we want to be like Singapore, but we forget
why Singapore is Singapore today. It is because they
work as Singaporeans who respect your race, religion,

language and culture; they respect each other and is like a
platform which allows everybody to move on. | am
extremely grateful that in this year's Presidential Election,
nobody is taking notice of race, religion or language;
people are talking about national issues. Some people are
trying to twist all that and take advantage, but people are
ignoring it. People want someone who can drive this
country forward, develop this nation and who can give a
better level of life for everyone while creating a safe and
secure future.

It is a good step. | think we should build on that and
not go backward on that. I know, some people will lose
out on it because no longer, their divisive agenda is
sellable and they are upset about it. But, as a country, we
should be proud that people are coming together and are
talking about national issues and not about racial, ethnic
or other artificial issues which have divided us for such a
long period of time.

Sir, | am also grateful that at the Committee on
Parliamentary Business, we have agreed to pass these
good laws without a Division. And, we will continue to
come up with such other laws. Law is a process which
continues to evolve. You need to have standing
committees looking into all these laws because no law is
perfect. If you wait for a perfect law to come, it would
never come.

679 2024 සැප්තැම්බර්‌ 03 680

ගරු ඇමතිතුමනි, අද දින ඉදිරිපත්‌ කළ ශ්‍රී ලංකාවේ සන්‍යය.
සමගිය සහ ප්‍රතිසන්ධානය සඳහා වන කොමිෂන්‌ සභාව පනන්‌
කෙටුම්පතෙහි දඬුවම්‌ දීමේ විධිවිධාන නැහැ කියලා ඔබතුමා
කිව්වා. එතැන කාරණා දෙකක්‌ තිබෙනවා. වරදක්‌ කරලා
තිබෙනවා නම්‌, ඊට දඬුවම්‌ ලැබිය යුතුයි කියලා ඔබතුමා කිව්වා.
හැබැයි, මේ පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතේ ඒක නැහැ, මම පිළිගන්නවා.
හැබැයි, මේ පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතට අනුව අපරාධ සම්බන්ධ සාක්ෂි
එකතු කරනවා.

ඕඔබතුමාම අද ගෙනාපු අනෙක්‌ පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතෙන්‌ විදේශ
නඩු තීන්දු ලංකාවට අදාළ කර ගන්න ප්‍රතිපාදන තිබෙනවා. මේ
සාක්ෂි මත පිට රටකදී නඩු දැම්මොත්‌ ඒ නඩු තීන්දු අපට අදාළ
වෙන්න අවශ්‍ය ඒ දෙක අතර සම්බන්ධය ඔබතුමන්ලා හදලා
තිබෙනවා. එක පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතක ඒ නතත්ත්චය නැහැ. අනෙක්‌
පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතේ තිබෙනවා.

ඒ වාගේම මේකටත්‌ උත්තර දෙන්න, ගරු ඇම්තිතුමනි. 1983
ඉඳුන්‌ කරපු අපරාධ ගැන හොයනවා නම්‌, ඒ සාක්ෂි එකතු කරනවා
නම්‌, වන්දි ගෙවනවා නම්‌, මේකෙන්‌ 1988-89 කාලය අයින්‌
කරලා තිබෙන්නේ ඇයි? 1988-89 කාලයේ කරපු අපරාධ මේ
සන්‍යයට අදාළ නොවන්නේ ඇයි? ඒවාත්‌ මිනිස්‌ ජීවිත නොවෙයිද?
ඒචා තරුණ ජීවිත නොවෙයිද? ඒ අම්මලා දුක්‌ වෙන්නේ නැද්ද?
ඇයි ඉතින්‌ ඒ කාලය ඉවන්‌ කරලා තිබෙන්නේ?

ගරු ජනාධිපති නීතිඥ එම්‌.යු.එම්‌. අලි සබ්රි මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு சனாதிபதி சட்டத்தரணி எம்‌.யூ.எம்‌. அலி சப்ரி)

(The Hon. M.U.M. Ali Sabry, PC)

ඔබතුමා මේක පටලවා ගෙන තිබෙන්නේ, ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමා. අද
ගෙනාපු පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතෙන්‌ කරන්න පුළුවන්‌, දික්කසාද නඩු
අපේ රටේ ලියාපදිංචි කරන්න පුළුවන්‌ එකයි. මුදල්‌ අය කරන්න
තිබෙන දේවල්‌ සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌ අපරාධ නඩු ගෙනෙන්න බැහැ.
ප්‍රශ්නය අහන්න ඉස්සෙල්ලා පොඞ්ඩක්‌ කියවන්න. ඔබතුමා ඒකයි,
මේකයි පටලවා ගෙන. කුමන්ත්‍රණ තිබෙනවා කියලා හිතුවොන්‌
හැම දේම පෙනෙන්නේ කුමන්ත්‍රණ විධියට. එහෙම කිසිම
අදාළත්වයක්‌ නැහැ.

දෙවැනි කාරණය මෙයයි. එම පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පත මඟින්‌ කිසිම
නඩුවක්‌ දාන්න බැහැ. වරදක්‌ කළොත්‌ සාමාන්‍ය නීතිය යටතේ
දඬුවම්‌ කරන්න එපා යැ. ඒක වරදක්ද? වරදක්‌ කළොත්‌ නිකම්‌
ඉන්න පුළුවන්ද? ඒක නිසා මේකෙන්‌ අපි සන්‍යය විතරක්‌ සොයලා

ගරු ගෙවිඳු කුමාරතුංග මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு கெவிந்து குமாரதுங்க)

(The Hon. Gevindu Cumaratunga)

1988-89 කාලය ගැනන්‌ හොයන්න.

ගරු ජනාධිපති නීතිඥ එම්‌.යු.එම්‌. අලි සබ්රි මහතා

ගරු රාජ්‍ය ඇමතිතුමනි, ඒචා අභ්‍යන්තර ප්‍රශ්න. මෛන්‍රීපාල

ඔක්කොම ඔබතනුමන්ලාගේ පක්ෂයේ 11151114] [00111125. ඒවා
ඔබතුමන්ලා විසඳා ගන්න ඕනෑ. මේ සභාවට ඇවිල්ලා අපට ඒවා

ගරු නියෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුමනි, මම මුල ඉඳන්ම කිව්වේ

[1.25 p.m.]

ගරු වඩිවේල්‌ සුරේෂ්‌ මහතා (කම්කරු රාජ්‍ය අමාතාතුමා)

(மாண்புமிகு வடிவேல்‌ சுரேஷ்‌ - தொழில்‌ இராஜாங்க

அமைச்சர்‌)

(The Hon. Vadivel Suresh - State Minister of Labour)

Hon. Deputy Speaker, today, we are debating the
National Minimum Wage of Workers (Amendment) Bill
to increase the minimum wage of the private sector
employees.

Sir, this Bill, the Second Reading of which is
scheduled to be taken up, proposes Amendments to the
National Minimum Wage of Workers Act, No. 3 of 2016.
The primary goal of this Amendment is to raise the
current national minimum wage for private sector
employees from Rs. 12,500 to Rs. 17,500. More than
three million of the Sri Lankan workforce is currently
employed in the private sector.

Presently, several key legal frameworks are in place
to determine wages of these workers. Notably, wages are
set by the decision of the Wages Boards established
under the Wages Boards Ordinance, No. 27 of 1941.
Additionally, wages are also set through collective
agreements between employers and employees. Sir, the
Wages Boards Ordinance determines wages only to
industries for which Wages Boards have been
established. Currently, Wages Boards have been set for
44 such industries. However, the decisions of the Wages
Boards do not cover all the employees in the private
sector in Sri Lanka.

Prior to the National Minimum Wage of Workers Act,
No. 03 of 2016, wages for employees, particularly of
those who were covered under the Shop and Office
Employees (Regulation of Employment and
Remuneration) Act, were primarily determined through
agreements made at the time of recruitment of
employees. Although unionized workers have been able
to get their wages raised, the majority of the private
sector workers are unable to negotiate with their
employers to get their wages increased. In addition to
that, the high rate of unemployment and prevalence of
unskilled workers further hinder their ability to negotiate
for better salaries upon hiring. That is why the
Government intervened through legal provisions to
protect these vulnerable workers by mandating wage
increases.


--- Page 61 ---
691 2024 සැප්තැම්බර්‌ 03 692

Sir, for the first time in Sri Lanka, the national
minimum wage for all employees working in the private
sector was introduced through a statutory law effective
from 1* January, 2016. Initially, that set a minimum
monthly wage of Rs. 10,000 for workers and a minimum
of Rs. 400 for daily-wage workers and that amount was
set based on the official Poverty Line of Rs. 6,117 at that
time. By an Amendment to this Act in 2021, the
minimum monthly wage was increased from Rs. 10,000
to Rs. 12,500 and the daily wage from Rs. 400 to Rs. 500,
effective from August, 2021. Currently, the private sector
employers are required to pay a minimum monthly wage
of Rs. 16,000 to workers, which includes the national
minimum wage of Rs. 12,500 and the budgetary
allowance of Rs. 3,500, as mandated by the Budgetary
Relief Allowance of Workers Act, No. 36 of 2005 and the
Budgetary Relief Allowance of Workers Act, No. 4 of
2016.

Sir, due to the recent economic crisis, the cost of
living has increased significantly. Yet, there has been no
corresponding raise in the minimum wage of the private
sector employees since 2021. It has been observed that
many employers currently pay a minimum wage of Rs.
16,000 to employees in the security service, cleaning
service and small shops and offices. This amount is
insufficient, given the current cost of living. According to
the Department of Census and Statistics, the Official
Poverty Line has risen to Rs. 16, 326 by May, 2024. This
indicates that the national minimum wage for private
sector employees is below the Official Poverty Line.

Sir, this Amendment aims to raise the current monthly
national minimum wage from Rs. 12,500 to Rs. 17, 500
and the daily minimum wage from Rs. 500 to Rs. 700.
With this increase, the employers will be legally required
to pay a minimum of Rs. 21,000 to the private sector
employees, which includes the increased Rs. 17,500 and
the Budgetary Relief Allowance of Rs. 3,500. Raising the
national minimum wage to Rs. 21,000 is also likely to
increase the contribution percentage to the Employees’
Provident Fund and the Employees’ Trust Fund, which
have been established for workers’ social security.
Additionally, employers will be legally required to base
workers' gratuity calculation on this new minimum wage,
resulting in higher gratuity payments for employees. This
Amendment is both timely and essential. Therefore, | call
on everyone to lend their support for the approval of this
Amendment.

கெளரவ பிரதிச்‌ சபாநாயகர்‌ அவர்களே, மலையகத்திலும்‌
நாட்டின்‌ ஏனைய பகுதிகளிலும்‌ இருக்கின்ற பலர்‌ இன்று
தனியார்துறையிலே - கடைகளிலும்‌ தொழிற்சாலைகளிலும்‌ -
கடமையாற்றி வருகின்றார்கள்‌. அவர்களின்‌ குறைந்தபட்ச
12,500 ரூபாயிலிருந்து 17,000 ரூபாயாக
அதிகரிக்கப்படுகின்றது. அதாவது, அடிப்படைச்‌
5,000 ரூபாயினை அதிகரிப்பதோடு, வரவு செலவுத்‌

ஒரு. தோட்டத்‌ தொழிலாளி அல்லது வேறு தொழில்‌
செய்பவர்கள்‌ பெற வேண்டும்‌ என்பதைத்‌ தொழில்‌ அமைச்சின்‌

ேோாபர்‌(சயிலே கலந்துரையாடப்பட்டிருக்கிறது. ஆகவே,
ஒவ்வொரு வேலைதருநரும்‌ கம்பனி அல்லது கடைச்‌ சொந்தக்‌

எனக்குக்‌ கிடைத்த பாரியதொரு வரப்பிரசாதமாகவும்‌
பாக்கியமாகவும்‌ இதனை நான்‌ கருதுகின்றேன்‌.

அந்தத்‌ தொழிலாளர்‌ வர்க்கத்தைச்‌ சார்ந்தவன்‌ என்ற
வகையிலே, அவர்களுடைய சம்பள உயர்வு சம்பந்தமாக

சம்பள நிர்ணய சபை
வகையில்‌, தனியார்துறையில்‌ வேலை செய்யும்‌ அனைத்துத்‌
தொழிலாளர்களினதும்‌ சம்பளத்தை அரசாங்கம்‌ அதிகரிப்ப
தென்பது வரவேற்கத்தக்கதாக இருக்கின்றது. ஆகவே, இந்த
சம்பள உயர்வு சட்டமாக்கப்பட்டு, அனைத்து தனியார்‌
அதனைப்‌
ஏற்பாடுகள்‌ மேற்கொள்ளப்பட்டிருக்கின்றன. அது தவிர,

நாட்‌ ஊம்‌ gratuity
பாரியதொரு தொழில்‌ பாதுகாப்பு - தொழில்‌ காப்புறுதி -
இதிலே உறுதி செய்யப்படுகின்றது என்பதையும்‌ நான்‌ இந்தச்‌
சந்தர்ப்பத்திலே தெரிவித்துக்‌ கொள்கின்றேன்‌.

கெளரவ பிரதிச்‌ சபாநாயகர்‌ அவர்களே, இன்று குற்றவியல்‌
(திருத்தம்‌)
மீதான விவாதமும்‌ நடைபெறும்‌ வேளையில்‌, நான்‌ எமது
அரசியலமைப்பை மீறும்‌ குற்றவாளிகள்‌ சம்பந்தமாகவே பேச

விழைகின்றேன்‌. ஜனாதிபதித்‌ தேர்தல்‌ நடைபெறவிருக்கின்ற

மக்களுக்கு மாத்திரமல்ல, பகுதி
மக்களுக்கும்‌ பல உண்மைகளை வெளிப்படுத்தும்‌ நிலையை
ஏற்படுத்தியுள்ளது. ஆகவே, இவ்வுரையாற்றுவதில்‌ எனக்கு
மகிழ்வாகும்‌. அதாவது, நடைபெறவிருக்கின்ற ஜனாதிபதித்‌

உரையாற்றுவதை நான்‌

எனக்கு மகிழ்வளிக்கும்‌ தருணமாகும்‌.

நடத்தப்படவில்லை? அதற்கான காரணம்‌ என்ன? ஆளும்‌

ஏற்பட்ட சட்டச்‌ சிக்கலா? அப்படியாயின்‌, அந்தச்‌ சட்டச்‌
சிக்கல்‌ ஏற்படுவதற்குக்‌ அதற்கு யார்‌

விரும்பவில்லை. 1987ஆம்‌ ஆண்டு கைச்சாத்திடப்பட்ட
இந்திய - இலங்கை ஒப்பந்தத்தின்‌ பிரகாரம்‌ இலங்கை அரசிய
லமைப்பின்‌ 13ஆவது திருத்தமாக எமது சட்டவாக்க மீயுயர்‌

காரணம்‌ என்ன?

சபையான பாராளுமன்றத்தால்‌ முறைப்படி நிறைவேற்றப்பட்டு
பிரிக்கமுடியாத ஒரு
மாகாண சபைகள்‌ அமைந்துள்ளது. எமது நாட்டின்‌ ஜனாதிபதி,
பிரதமர்‌, பாராளுமன்ற உறுப்பினர்கள்‌ அனைவரும்‌ தமது

எமது அரசியலமைப்பின்‌ பாகமாக

பதவிப்‌ பிரமாண வைபவத்தின்போது, இலங்கை ஜனநாயக
சோசலியக்‌ கூடியரசின்‌ அரசியலமைப்புக்குப்‌ பற்றுறுதியோடு
இருப்பதாகவும்‌
அரசியலமைப்பை உறுதியாகக்‌ காப்பதாகவும்‌ உறுதியுரை
செய்து இந்த உறுதியுரையை
இதுவரை ஆட்சி செய்த ஆட்சியாளர்கள்‌ கடைப்பிடித்‌
துள்ளார்களா? அவ்வாறு கடைப்பிடித்திருந்தார்களாயின்‌ இந்த

பணிபுரிவதாகவும்‌ அதற்கு விசுவாசமாக

பதவியேற்கின்றார்கள்‌.

நாட்டில்‌ பொருளாதாரப்‌ பிரச்சினை தோற்றம்‌ பெற்றிருக்காது;
நீண்ட வரிசைகள்‌ - 0ப6ப6 - உதயமாகியிருக்காது. ஏன்‌,
ஏற்பட்டிருக்காது. தெரிவு
செய்யப்பட்ட அரசுத்‌ தலைவரும்‌ பிரதமரும்‌ பின்‌ கதவால்‌ ஓடி

'அரகலய'கூட மக்களால்‌
ஒளிந்துகொள்ளும்‌ தேவையும்‌ வந்திருக்காது. நீண்ட காலமாக
மாகாண சபைத்‌ தேர்தல்கள்‌ நடத்தப்படவில்லை. வட மாகாண
சபைத்‌ தேர்தல்‌ 2018ஆம்‌ ஆண்டு நடைபெற்றிருக்க வேண்டும்‌.
கிழக்கு ஆண்டு
நடைபெற்றிருக்க வேண்டும்‌. அதையண்மித்த காலங்களில்‌

மாகாண சபைத்‌ தேர்தல்‌ 2017ஆம்‌

தென்‌ மற்றும்‌ ஏனைய மாகாண
வேண்டும்‌.

மாகாண

சபைத்‌ தேர்தல்களும்‌
நடைபெற்றிருக்க மாறிமாறி வந்த
ஆட்சியாளர்கள்‌ சபைத்‌ தேர்தல்‌ தொடர்பாக
அக்கறையற்றவர்களாகவே இருந்தனர்‌. இதற்கு ஆளும்‌ கட்சி
மாத்திரமல்ல, எதிர்க்கட்சிகளும்‌ பொறுப்பேற்க வேண்டும்‌.

ஆனால்‌,

கெளரவ பிரதிச்‌ சபாநாயகர்‌ அவர்களே, கடந்த காலத்தில்‌
உள்ளூராட்சி சபைத்‌ தேர்தல்‌ தொடர்பாகத்‌ தேர்தல்‌ பிரகடனம்‌

செய்யப்பட்டு, வேட்பு மனுக்கள்‌ கோரப்பட்டு, அதன்‌ பின்னர்‌
அரசாங்கத்தின்‌ தோல்விப்‌ பயத்தைப்‌ பின்னால்‌ வைத்து,
பொருளாதாரப்‌ பிரச்சினையை முன்னால்‌ வைத்து அத்தேர்தல்‌
ஒத்திவைக்கப்பட்டது. இந்தத்‌ தேர்தல்‌ ஒத்திவைப்புத்‌ தொடர்‌
பாக நாட்டின்‌ எதிர்க்கட்சிகளும்‌ சிவில்‌ அமைப்புக்களும்‌ அரச
சார்பற்ற நிறுவனங்களும்‌ வெகுசன ஊடகங்களும்‌ காட்டிய
அக்கறையில்‌ ஒரு துளியையேனும்‌ மாகாண சபைத்‌
தேர்தல்கள்‌ தொடர்பாகக்‌ காட்டவில்லை. இதற்கான காரணம்‌,
மாகாண சபை அமைப்பும்‌ மாகாண சயைத்‌ தேர்தலும்‌
இலங்கை பிரிக்க முடியாத அம்சம்‌
என்பதைவிட, அது வடக்கு, கிழக்குத்‌ தமிழ்‌ மக்களுடைய

அரசியலமைப்பின்‌

பிரச்சினை என்பதாகவே தென்பகுதி அரசியல்‌ கட்சிகளும்‌

தென்பகுதி ஊடகங்களும்‌ தென்பகுதி மனித உரிமை
அமைப்புகளும்‌ அரச சார்பற்ற நிறுவனங்களும்‌
கருதுகின்றமையாகும்‌.

உள்ளூராட்சித்‌ தேர்தல்‌ ஒத்திவைக்கப்பட்டமை

தொடர்பாகத்‌ தங்களது அடிப்படை உரிமை மீறப்பட்டதாக
நீதி கோரி உச்ச நீதிமன்றம்‌ சென்ற அரசியல்‌ கட்சிகள்‌, மனித
உரிமைச்‌ செயற்பாட்டாளர்கள்‌ மாகாண சபைத்‌ தேர்தல்‌
நடத்தப்படாததால்‌ தங்களது அடிப்படை
மீறப்பட்டதாக உணரவில்லை. எதற்கெடுத்தாலும்‌ சட்ட
வியாக்கியானம்‌ கொடுக்கும்‌ சட்டவியலாளர்கள்‌ இதன்மூலம்‌
தமது அடிப்படை உரிமைகள்‌ மீறப்பட்டதாக உணரவில்லை.

உரிமை

மாகாண சபைத்‌ தேர்தல்‌ நடத்தப்படாமை தொடர்பாகச்‌
சட்டத்தரணிகள்‌ சங்கமும்‌ மூச்சுவிடவில்லை. ஏனென்றால்‌,
மாகாண சபை என்பது வடக்கு, கிழக்குத்‌ தமிழர்‌ தொடர்பான
பிரச்சினை என்பதுவே இவர்கள்‌ அனைவரதும்‌ கருத்துருவாக்க
மாகும்‌. இது எமது அரசியலமைப்பின்‌ ஒரு பகுதி என்பது
இவர்களால்‌ உணரப்படவில்லை. தமிழில்‌ ஒரு பழமொழி
யுள்ளது, “தனக்குத்‌ தனக்கென்றால்‌ சுளகு படக்கு படக்கு
என்று அடிக்குமாம்‌” என்று. இது யாருக்குப்‌ பொருந்துமோ
தெரியாது. ஆனால்‌, தென்பகுதி அரசியல்‌ தலைவர்களுக்குச்‌
சாலப்‌ பொருந்தும்‌.

வேட்பாளர்களது
வேட்பாளர்களின்‌

ஜனாதிபதித்‌ தேர்தல்‌ சூறாவளியும்‌
விஞ்ஞாபனமும்‌ வெளிவந்துவிட்டது.
பரப்புரைகள்‌ வேகமாக நடக்கின்றன. அவர்களுடைய விஞ்ஞா
பனமும்‌ பரப்புரையும்‌ வைக்கின்றது.
1987ஆம்‌ ஆண்டு கொண்டுவரப்பட்ட பதின்மூன்றாவது
அரசியலமைப்புச்‌ சீர்திருத்தம்‌ எமது அரசியலமைப்பின்‌ பிரிக்க
முடியாத அங்கமாக மாறியது. ஆனால்‌, அதனை முழுமையாக
அமுல்படுத்துவதில்‌ இந்த நாட்டின்‌ அரசுகளும்‌ அதனை
அமுல்படுத்த வலியுறுத்துவதில்‌ இங்குள்ள எதிர்க்கட்சிகளும்‌
அக்கறை காட்டவில்லை. 1948இன்‌  சுதந்திரத்துக்குப்‌
பின்னரான எமது நாட்டின்‌ அரசியல்‌ வரலாற்றில்‌ நாம்‌

என்னை வியக்க

நோக்கக்கூடிய விசேட அம்சம்‌ என்னவென்றால்‌, ஆளும்கட்சி
எத்தகைய திட்டங்களைக்கொண்டு வந்தாலும்‌, அது மக்கள்‌
நலன்‌ சார்ந்த திட்டங்களாக இருந்தாலும்கூட, பல்வேறு
வியாக்கியானங்களைக்‌ கூறி அதனை எதிர்ப்பதே எதிர்க்கட்சி
களின்‌ சம்பிரதாயக்‌ கடமையாக இருப்பதுதான்‌. ஆனால்‌,
பதின்மூன்றாவது திருத்தத்தை
முழுமையாக அமுல்படுத்தாது, அதனை எவ்வாறு கருவில்‌
அழிக்கலாம்‌, எவ்வாறு குறைப்‌ பிரசவமாக்கலாம்‌ என்பதில்‌
ஆளும்‌ எதிர்க்கட்சிக்குமிடையில்‌
எழுதப்படாத புரிந்‌ துணர்வு ஒப்பந்தம்‌ உள்ளதா? என்ற ஐயம்‌
எனக்கு உள்ளது.

எமது அரசியலமைப்பின்‌

மட்டும்‌ கட்சிக்கும்‌

எதிர்வரும்‌ ஜனாதிபதித்‌ தேர்தலில்‌ போட்டியிடும்‌
வேட்பாளர்களின்‌, குறிப்பாகச்‌ சுயேட்சை வேட்பாளர்‌ ரணில்‌
விக்கிரமசிங்ஹ, ஐக்கிய மக்கள்‌ சக்தி வேட்பாளர்‌ சஜித்‌
பிரேமதாஸ, இன்று தேசிய மக்கள்‌ சக்தியாக முகம்‌ காட்டும்‌
அன்றைய ஐஐ கி cadGas வேட்பாளர்‌ தோழர்‌ அநுர

695 2024 සැප්තැම්බර්‌ 03 696

குமார திஸாநாயக்க ஆகியோரது விஞ்ஞாபனத்தில்‌ வடக்கு,
கிழக்கு வாழ்‌ தமிழ்‌ மக்களது பிரச்சினைகள்‌ தொடர்பாகக்‌
குறிப்பிடப்பட்டிருப்‌ கிழக்கில்‌
அவர்களது பிரசாரங்களையும்‌ அவதானிக்கும்போது நான்‌

பவைகளையும்‌ வடக்கு,
உண்மையில்‌ எனது உடம்பைக்‌ கிள்ளிப்‌ பார்க்கிறேன்‌; எனது
கேட்கும்‌ திறனைச்‌ சந்தேகிக்கின்றேன்‌.. இவர்களது
உரைகளைப்‌ பத்திரிகைகளில்‌ வாசிக்கும்போது எனது
கட்புலனை ஜஐயுறுகின்றேன்‌. அந்தளவுக்கு இவர்களது தேர்தல்‌
விஞ்ஞாபனங்களும்‌ தேர்தல்‌ பரப்புரைகளும்‌ அமைந்துள்ளன.
பதின்மூன்றாவது அரசியலமைப்புச்‌ சீர்திருத்தம்‌ தொடர்பான
இவர்களது பரப்புரைகள்‌ மற்றும்‌ தேர்தல்‌ விஞ்ஞாபனங்களில்‌
குறிப்பிட்டுள்ளவைகள்‌ தொடர்பாக, குறித்த அரசியலமைப்புச்‌
சீர்திருத்தம்‌ ஏற்பட்ட 1987ஆம்‌ ஆண்டிலிருந்து இதுவரை
இவர்களது கட்சி மாநாடுகளிலோ அல்லது பாராளுமன்றத்தில்‌
வடக்கு, கிழக்குப்‌ பிரச்சினைகள்‌ தொடர்பான விவாதங்கள்‌
நிகழ்கின்றபோதோ தமது உரைகளில்‌
கூறியுள்ளார்களா? ஏதோ நேற்றுத்தான்‌ பதின்மூன்றாவது
அரசியலமைப்புச்‌ சீர்திருத்தம்‌ கொண்டுவரப்பட்டது போன்றும்‌

எதையாவது

நாளை அதனை அமுல்படுத்துவதாகவும்‌ தமது
பரப்புரைகளிலும்‌ தேர்தல்‌ விஞ்ஞாபனத்திலும்‌ இவர்கள்‌
குறிப்பிடுவதிலிருந்து நாம்‌ இவர்களைப்‌ பற்றிப்‌ பூரண
தெளிவடைந்துள்ளோம்‌.

இத்தகைய சூழ்நிலையில்தான்‌, வெல்ல முடியாதெனத்‌
தெரிந்தும்‌ எமது பொதுப்‌ பிரதிநிதியாக முன்னாள்‌ பாராளு
மன்ற உறுப்பினர்‌ ஒருவரை வடக்கு, கிழக்குவாழ்‌ தமிழ்‌
மக்களின்‌ ஏகோபித்த ஆதரவுடன்‌ ஜனாதிபதி வேட்பாளராக

[අ.භා. 1.45]

ගරු චින්තක අමල්‌ මායාදුන්න මහතා
(மாண்புமிகு சிந்தக அமல்‌ மாயாதுன்ன)
(The Hon. Chinthaka Amal Mayadunna)

මූලාසනාරූඞ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි, අද දිනයේ අපරාධ නඩු විධාන
සංග්‍රහය (සංශෝධන) පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පත සහ විදේශ නඩු තීන්දු
අනෞ්‍යෝනාව පිළිගැනීම, ලියාපදිංචි කිරීම සහ බලාත්මක කිරීම
පිළිබඳ පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතන්‌, සේවකයන්ගේ ජාතික අවම චේතනය
(සංශෝධන) පනත්‌ කෙටුමිපතත්‌ පාර්ලිමේන්තුවට ඉදිරිපත්‌ කර
තිබෙනවා. මේ අවස්ථාවේදී මම මුලින්ම සඳහන්‌ කළ යුතුයි,
අපරාධ නඩු විධාන සංග්‍රහය හරහා අප කළ යුතු ලොකු
කාර්යභාරයක්‌ තිබෙන බව.

මූලාසනාරූඞ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි, පසුගිය කාලය තුළ අපි දැක්කා

කාලයක්‌ තිබෙනවා.

[1.50 p.m.]

ගරු එම්‌.ඒ. සුමන්තිරන්‌ මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு எம்‌.ஏ. சுமந்திரன்‌)

(The Hon. M.A. Sumanthiran)

Hon. Presiding Member, | would like to congratulate
the Hon. Minister of Justice, Prison Affairs and
Constitutional Reforms for bringing in the Reciprocal
Recognition, Registration and Enforcement of Foreign
Judgments Bill. What we had all these years was a very
old piece of legislation, which was not useful or adequate
for current purposes and often, we had difficulty in
recognizing foreign judgments. | am glad that this Bill is
being taken up for debate today because we should have
kept up with the times, but, at least now, a new piece of
legislation is being introduced.

While we are on that, I must say that there are several
pieces of legislation that have been introduced in this
House in the last 20 months or so mostly by your
predecessor and former senior, who is a Presidential
candidate now, the Hon. (Dr.) Wijeyadasa Rajapakshe,
President’s Counsel. He claims that there had been about
75 or so new laws introduced. We have not kept count of
that. Nevertheless, law reform is an important issue and
modernizing our laws is an essential feature and | am
glad that some of the laws that were brought in were
necessary and served to fulfil a long-felt need.

Yet for all, today, | stand here disappointed that the
only piece of legislation that ought to have been passed
much earlier, in fact, in the last Parliament itself, to clear
the legal block that had been created by the Amendment
that was brought in 2017 to the Provincial Council
Elections Act has not been taken up today. In that
Parliament itself, | brought a Private Members’ Bill to
remove that legal tangle and enable Provincial Council
Elections to be held under the system that existed prior to
that Amendment. Unfortunately, that did not see the light
of day and then, there was a change. | brought in the Bill
all over again a second time. Then, Parliament was
prorogued and | had to bring it a third time. But, what 1
brought the third time survived until today. It was
actually sent to the Attorney-General; he took his own
time and thereafter, it was gazetted. The Bill was read the

699 2024 සැප්තැම්බර්‌ 03 700

First time and then, there were two petitioners who went
to the Supreme Court on that. They cited me as a
respondent and | appeared in person. Then, the Supreme
Court gave its Determination stating that subject to the
change of wording the Supreme Court itself suggested, it
could be passed with a simple majority.

Thereafter, the Bill was taken up for Second Reading
after a lapse of several months. After President Ranil
Wickremesinghe took office, he promised that several
provisions of the devolution arrangements that we find
today in the Constitution would be implemented. He
started a process in December, 2022, an All-Party
Conference. Then, he had five consecutive meetings with
our party, the Tamil National Alliance. We attended all of
those despite several parties boycotting same. We wanted
to co-operate with that effort. He claimed that we would
resolve the outstanding Tamil national question before the
75" Independence Day, which fell on the 04" of
February, 2023. But, that did not happen. He kept
promising all of this for a long period of time and as the
Presidential Election neared, he again started discussions
with us on the old promises and one of those things that
we told him was, “Provincial Council Elections must be
held. It cannot be delayed like this forever.” He agreed.
There was no time to bring in an amendment from the
Government side to that Act and my Amendment was
awaiting to be taken up for Second Reading. So, he
agreed that that could be taken up and passed, and he
even said that this is the first time that, under this
Constitution, a Private Members’ Bill would actually
become a law. And, he kept his promise. When the
Second Reading of the Bill was taken up, there was no
call for a debate, there was no call for a Division and it
was passed. Thereafter, since it was a Private Members’
Bill, it was referred to the Legislative Standing
Committee. The Legislative Standing Committee met
twice, made the necessary Amendments that had been
suggested by the Supreme Court and gave its Report to
this House on the 21* of August, last month. At that time,
it was agreed that the Third Reading would be taken up
today. The Third Reading is a mere formality of
presenting the Report of the Legislative Standing
Committee and accepting it. Any Member of the House, if
he wanted it, could have asked for a Division at the Third
Reading. So, it was up to the House to either accept it or
reject it. But, something else intervened in between.

 

The Central Working Committee of the Nankai Tamil
Arasu Kadchi met two days ago, on Sunday, the 01° of
September in Vavuniya and after a long deliberation of
five hours - that was the fifth meeting at which we were
considering these matters - we took a definite decision not
to support the so-called Tamil common candidate. Ours is
the only Tamil party which has taken that courageous
decision not to support the so-called Tamil common
candidate. We have been branded traitors, we have been
called names, but for the sake of our people and for the
sake of the country, we took that courageous decision
with an overwhelming majority. Then, at the end of the
meeting, before the resolution was passed, those who
dissented were asked and they said, “No, we do not need
a vote. It can be accepted.” So, it was accepted
wholeheartedly without a division. That is what our

Central Committee decided. When we took that decision,
we also took a decision that, as a responsible political
party, which is the main Tamil political party, it is our
bounden duty to inform our people as to whom they
should vote.

We cannot leave it open; we have to give guidance to
our people. On that account, we considered the relative
merits of the manifestos presented by three main
candidates and decided unanimously to support the Hon.
Leader of the Opposition Sajith Premadasa. That decision
could have gone any way. But, that is a decision taken by
our party to give guidance to our people as to how they
should vote. They may follow it; they may not follow it.
But, something strange happened thereafter. Until that
point, the President and the Government were agreeable
to the passage of this piece of legislation; they were
agreeable that it should be taken up for the Third Reading
today. But, all that changed and yesterday, at the Meeting
of the Committee on Parliamentary Business, I was told
that it could not be taken up today. That is what you call
“a political witch-hunt”; that is what you call “acting
without principles’. I told the Hon. (Dr.) Susil
Premajayantha at the Meeting yesterday that a large
number of Tamil people are very sympathetic to the
President on various basis, that he still had a lot of
support. But, by this one act, he has exposed his true self
to the people.

இந்த ஒரு நடவடிக்கையின்மூலம்‌ தான்‌ யார்‌ என்பதை
அவர்‌ திரும்பவும்‌ மக்களுக்கு நிரூபித்திருக்கின்றார்‌. வாய்ச்‌
சொல்லால்‌ பலவிதமான வாக்குறுதிகள்‌ கொடுப்பதும்‌, அதை
அமுல்நடத்துவதைப்போலக்‌ காட்டுவதும்‌, இறுதித்‌
தறுவாயிலே அதற்கான கடைசி அடியெடுப்பைச்‌ செய்யாமல்‌
விடுவதும்‌ ரணில்‌ விக்கிரமசிங்ஹ அவர்களின்‌ சுபாவம்‌
என்பதை இந்தத்‌ தருணத்திலும்‌
தனக்கு வாக்களிக்காமல்‌ விடுகின்ற தீர்மானத்தைப்‌ பிரதான

காண்பித்திருக்கின்றார்‌.

தமிழ்க்‌ கட்சி எடுத்திருப்பதன்‌ காரணமாக, தமிழ்‌ மக்களைத்‌

அரைகுறைத்‌
மாகாண

தண்டிக்கவேண்டுமேன்று,
இருந்தாலும்கூட இருக்கின்ற
நடத்தவிடாமல்‌ பண்ணுவதற்காக இப்படியாக மிக மோசமான
ஒரு. நடத்தையிலே ரணில்‌ விக்கிரமசிங்ஹ அவர்கள்‌
இன்றைக்கு இறங்கியிருக்கின்றார்‌. இந்த
நடத்தையின்மூலம்‌, கடந்த ஞாயிற்றுக்கிழமை 1ஆம்‌ திகதி
தமிழரசுக்‌ கட்சியினராகிய நாங்கள்‌ அவருக்கு
ஆதரவளிப்பதில்லையென்று எடுத்த தீர்மானம்‌
சரியானதென்று நிரூபணமாகின்றது.

தீர்வாக
சபைகளை

அவருடைய

அதேநேரம்‌, பிரதான எதிர்க்கட்சித்‌ தலைவருக்கு நாங்கள்‌
ஆதரவு கொடுக்கின்றபோது அவருக்கும்‌ இதனை ஓர்‌
எச்சரிக்கையாகச்‌ சொல்லிவைக்க விரும்புகின்றேன்‌. அதாவது,
அவர்‌ கொடுத்திருக்கின்ற வாக்குறுதிகளோடு எங்களுடன்‌
இணங்குகின்ற விடயங்களை முழுமையாக நிறைவேற்ற
வேண்டும்‌. இல்லையென்றால்‌ இந்த நாடு அழிவுப்‌
பாதைக்குள்‌ செல்லும்‌! சென்ற தடவையும்‌ எங்களுடைய
மக்களில்‌ அவருக்கு
வாக்களித்திருந்தார்கள்‌. அதுபோல்‌ இந்தத்‌ தடவையும்‌ தமிழ்‌
மக்கள்‌ எதிர்க்கட்சித்‌ தலைவருக்கு வாக்களிப்பார்கள்‌. ஆனால்‌,

பெரும்பான்மையானவர்கள்‌

நாடு பூராவும்‌ அவர்‌ வெளிப்படையாகச்‌ சொல்லியிருக்கின்ற

விடயங்கள்‌ நடைமுறைப்படுத்தப்பட வேண்டும்‌.
இல்லையென்றால்‌ இது பாரதூரமான விளைவுகளை
ஏற்படுத்தும்‌ என்ற எச்சரிக்கையோடு எனது பேச்சை

முடித்துக்கொள்கின்றேன்‌. நன்றி.

ගරු මුලාසනාරූඤ මන්ත්‍රීතුමා

(மாண்புமிகு தலைமைதாங்கும்‌ உறுப்பினர்‌ அவர்கள்‌)

(The Hon. Presiding Member)

ගරු බන්දුල ගුණවර්ධන අමාත්‍යතුමා. ඔබතුමාට මිනිත්තු 19ක
කාලයක්‌ තිබෙනවා.

[අ.භා. 2.04]

ගරු (ආචාර්ය) බන්දුල ගුණවර්ධන මහතා (ප්‍රවාහන හා

මහාමාර්ග අමාතා සහ ජනමාධා අමාන්‍යතුමා)

(மாண்புமிகு (கலாநிதி) பந்துல குணவர்தன - போக்குவரத்து

மற்றும்‌ நெடுஞ்சாலைகள்‌ அமைச்சரும்‌ வெகுசன ஊடக

அமைச்சரும்‌)

(The Hon. (Dr.) Bandula Gunawardana - Minister of

Transport and Highways and Minister of Mass Media)

මූලාසනාරූසඞ්‌ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනී, ගරු මධුර විතානගේ
ම්න්ත්‍රීතුමාගේ චීනාඩි 20ක කාලයන්‌ මට එකතු කරගන්න කිචිචා.

මූලාසනාරූසඞ්‌ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි, මට පෙර කථා කළ ගරු
සුමන්තිරන්‌ මන්ත්‍රීතුමා ගරු ජනාධිපතිතුමා පිළිබඳව කරපු සටහන
සාධාරණ නැති බව මම ප්‍රථමයෙන්ම ප්‍රකාශ කළ යුතු වෙනවා.
මක්නිසාද යන්‌, මේ ගරු සභාවේ සිදුවන කටයුතු
ජනාධිපතිතුමාගේ නියෝගය අනුව තීරණය නොවන නිසා.
ජනාධිපතිතුමාත්‌, අමාත්‍යවරුන්‌ යම්‌ යම්‌ කරුණු කලින්‌ සිදු
කරගන්න තීන්දු-තීරණ ගත්තත්‌, ඒ යොජනා 1741114111611141/
1115111655 (011111111166 එකට ඉදිරිපත්‌ වුණාම එහි සිටින ආණ්ඩු
පක්ෂයේතන්‌, විපක්ෂයේත්‌ සියලුදෙනාගේ එකඟතාව ඇතුව තමයි
ඒවා ඉදිරිපත්‌ කරන්න ඕනෑ. ගරු සුමන්තිරන්‌ මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි, ඒ බව

Committee එකේ ඊට වඩා ප්‍රමුඛනාව දිය යුතු කරුණු තිබෙනවා

අනාගතයත්‌, ජාතියේ පැවැත්මත්‌, ජාතීන්‌ අතර සමගියන්‌ ආදී
දේවල්‌ පදනම්‌ කරගෙන විශාල දැක්මක්‌ ඇතිව තම්යි එතුමාගේ
ප්‍රතිපත්ති ප්‍රකාශන සහ ආණ්ඩුවේ වැඩ පිළිවෙළ ක්‍රියාත්මක කරලා
තිබෙන්නේ කියලා. මෙය ලංකා ඉතිහාසයේ තීරණාත්මක

ස්තූතිවන්ත චෙමින්‌ මගේ වචන කීහිපය අවසන්‌ කරනවා.

ගරු මුලාසනාරූඤ මන්ත්‍රීතුමා

(மாண்புமிகு தலைமைதாங்கும்‌ உறுப்பினர்‌ அவர்கள்‌)

(The Hon. Presiding Member)

ගරු ඉරාන්‌ වික්‍රමරත්න මන්ත්‍රීතුමා. ඔබතුමාට මිනිත්තු 12ක
කාලයක්‌ තිබෙනවා.

[ අ.භා. 2.39]

ගරු ඉරාන්‌ වික්‍රමරත්න මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு இரான்‌ விக்கிரமரத்ன)

(The Hon. Eran Wickramaratne)

මූලාසනාරූසඞ්‌ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනී, මට මේ අවස්ථාව ලබා
දුන්නාට ස්තූතියි.

Sir, first of all, | would like to say something about the
Provincial Councils Elections (Amendment) Bill, which
had gone through its First Reading, the Second Reading
and was scheduled to be taken up in Parliament today for
its Third Reading. Unfortunately, it has not been
permitted to be taken up in Parliament today. It is very
unfortunate because, as we know, the provincial councils
have not been in operation for quite some time now and
that is really an issue about democracy. | do not agree
with the Hon. M.A. Sumanthiran when he says that the
Provincial Councils Elections (Amendment) Bill not

being taken up today is an injustice perpetrated on the
Tamil-speaking people because that is actually an
injustice perpetrated on all Sri Lankans.

Every Sri Lankan has a right to decide on his
particular provincial council, his local authority, the
Parliament and his President. We have been looking at a
very dangerous trend in this country, a trend of
authoritarianism. The United Nation’s report which has
just come out has shown that in the last two years, this
country has become more and more authoritarian. The
Supreme Court judgment given just a few days ago
specifically stated that the President of the country has no
right to postpone the Local Government Elections. He
has absolutely no right. We all are elected on a set of
tules, laws and on the Constitution and we have to
operate within that, whether you are the President, a
Cabinet Minister, a Member of Parliament or just a
citizen. That has been violated or in other words, the
supremacy or the sovereignty of the people has been
violated, according to that judgment. We believe in a
democratic way of life and leaders cannot say, "We
know what is best for everybody and we decide what is
best for everybody". That just cannot happen. The rule of
law has to be upheld and the Judiciary's verdicts have to
be upheld.

| heard some Hon. Members say that if the Provincial
Councils Elections (Amendment) Bill was taken up
today, it would have created some problems because we
are on the brink of an election. | do not agree with that at
all because these Bills go through a certain, long process:
the White Paper goes to the Attorney-General's
Department, then, to the Legal Draftsman’s Department
and after the First and the Second Readings, the Bill goes
to the Legislative Standing Committee and then only it
comes up for the Third Reading. That is how it is passed.
So, this particular Bill has also gone through that whole
process and that is why we completely object to what the
Government did today by not putting it before the House
for its Third Reading.

| heard another Hon. Member of Parliament say that
all the provincial councils were forced on us by India. I
do not know what kind of crap they come and speak here.
Are we really going to say that the Parliamentary system
was forced on us by the British people? I think we need
to grow up a little bit. These are global developments;
democracy is a global development. These are different
levels in a democracy. How those political systems -
parliamentary systems, presidential systems, devolved
systems and many different systems - operate differ. If
people feel that provincial councils are not suitable for
this country, then we can certainly have a Referendum
and when you have a Referendum, you are going to ask
the people in the province whether they need the
provincial council or not. You have to ask that from the
relevant people. We are not opposed to democracy, but
we are absolutely opposed to trying to postpone the
democratic framework in any way. Therefore, we
completely condemn the attempt made today to postpone
that legislation, which could have helped us to hold the
Provincial Council Elections by adopting the framework
that was in place earlier or based on the system that
existed earlier.

ප්‍රතිශත ප්‍රමාණයක්‌ ඉෂ්ට කරගෙන තිබෙනවා කියන එක ගැනයි

ඒක මිලියන 7කට ඉහළ ගිහිල්ලා තිබෙනවා. ඒ කියන්නේ මිනිස්සු
දුප්පත්‌ කරලා, දුප්පත්‌ කරලා අපට කියනවා ගිවිසුමක්‌ සාර්ථක කර
ගත්තා කියලා. ඒ නිසා මම හිතනවා ඒක දිහා එහෙම බලන්නට
බැහැ කියලා. අපි සමබරව ඒක ගැන බලන්න ඕනෑ. ආර්ථික

ස්ථාවරභාවයයි. ඉතින්‌ මිනිස්සු බිත්තියටම තල්ලු කරලායී ඒක
කරලා තිබෙන්නේ. අපි කිව්වා නම්‌ "අපි ඒක සංශෝධනය
කරනවා" කියලා, අනිචාර්යයෙන්ම සංශෝධනය කරනවා. ඒකේ
දෙකක්‌ නැහැ. අපි අඩු ආදායම්ලාභීන්‌ ආරක්ෂා කරනවා, ගැබිනි
මාතාවන්‌, කුඩා දරුවන්‌ අනිවාර්යෙන්ම ආරක්ෂා කරනවා.
ජ්‍යොෂ්ඨ පුරවැසියන්‌ අනිවාර්යයෙන්ම ආරක්ෂා කරනවා. අපි
දන්නවා ආදායමක්‌ අවශ්‍යයි කියලා. තිබෙන මිනිස්සුගෙන්‌
ගන්නවා, ඒකේ දෙකක්‌ නැහැ. අපි දන්නවා ආදායමක්‌ අවශ්‍යයි
කියලා. නමුත්‌, අපි මිනිස්සු දරිද්‍රතා රේඛාවෙන්‌ පහළට නොවෙයි
ඉහළටයි දාන්නේ. මිනිස්සු ඒ රේඛාවෙන්‌ ඉහළට දාන්න තමයි
අපේ වැඩ පිළිවෙළ තිබෙන්නේ.

සියලු පාර්ශ්වකරුවන්‌ සමඟ සාකච්ඡා කිරීමෙන්‌ අනතුරුව අපි
පොරොන්දු වෙලා තිබෙනවා පෞද්ගලික අංශයේ සේවා
නියුක්තිකයන්‌ සඳහා අවම මාසික වැටුප රුපියල්‌ 17,500 සිට
රුපියල්‌ 25,000 දක්වා හෝ සංශෝධනය කරන බවට. ඇයි, අපි
එහෙම කියන්නේ? රජයේ ලේඛන අනුව උද්ධමනය සියයට
70කින්‌ ඉහළට ගිහින්‌ තිබෙනවා, ආහාර උද්ධමනය සියයට
100කින්‌ ඉහළට ගිහිල්ලා තිබෙනවා. මම මේ ගැන එක තැනකදී
කියනකොට අම්මා කෙනෙක්‌ මා නතර කරලා කිව්වා, " මම
භිතන්නේ නැහැ ඔබතුමා මාර්කට්‌ එකට ගිහිල්ලා තිබෙනවා
කියලා" යනුවෙන්‌. මම ඇහුවා, ඇයි අම්මේ එහෙම කියන්නේ
කියලා. එතකොට ඒ අම්මා කිව්වා, "ඔබතුමා දන්නේ නැද්ද,
සමහර ආහාර ද්‍රව්‍යවල මිල දෙගුණයකින්‌ තුන්‌ ගුණයකින්‌ ඉහළට
ගිහිල්ලා නිබෙනවා. ඔබතුමා කියන්නේ සියයට 100ක්‌ චිතරයි,
එක්‌ ගුණයකින්‌ චීතරයි" කියලා. ඉතින්‌ මට ඒ අම්මා බැන්නා.

කරගෙන තිබෙන දේ වෙනුවෙන්‌ එතුමාගේ ප්‍රණාමය පුද කිරීමට
අවශ්‍ය බවත්‌, වසර දෙකකට පෙර ඇති චූ ආර්ථික අර්බුදයෙන්‌ පසු
රට තුළ ස්ථාවරත්වයක්‌ ඇති කීරීමට රනිල්‌ චික්‍රමසිංහ මහතා
සමන්‌ වී තිබෙන බවත්‌. මුලාසනාරූස ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි, ආසියානු
සංවර්ධන බැංකුවේ සභාපති මසට්සුගු අසකාචා මහතා 2024 මැයි
5වැනි දා කියලා තිබෙනවා, ආර්ථික සහ ක්‍රීයාකාරි සැලැස්ම
සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌ ශ්‍රී ලංකාව අත්‌ කරගෙන ඇති ප්‍රගතිය 86565
එතුමා ජනාධිපති රනිල්‌ වික්‍රමසිංහ මහතාට සහ ශ්‍රී ලංකා රජයට
ප්‍රශංසා කරන බව. ඒ වාගේම ජපාන විදේශ කටයුතු අමාත්‍ය
යො'කෝ කමීකාවා මහත්මිය 2024 මැයි 4වැනි දා කියලා
තිබෙනවා, ණය අර්බුදය විසඳීමට සහ ආර්ථික අර්බුදයෙන්‌ රට
ගොඩ ගැනීමේ ප්‍රතිසංස්කරණ කිරීමට රනිල්‌ වික්‍රමසිංහ මහතා
දක්වන නායකත්වය එතුමා අගය කරන බව. මේ කථා කරන්නේ,
රනිල්‌ චික්‍රමසිංහ ජනාධිපතිතුමා ගැන. ඒ වාගේම 2024 පෙබරවාරි
මාසයේ 19වැනි දා දකුණු සහ මධාම ආසියානු කටයුතු පිළිබඳ
එක්සත්‌ ජනපද සහකාර රාජ්‍ය ලේකම්‌ ඩොනල්ඩ්‌ ලූ මහතා
කියලා තිබෙනවා, එතුමා සේවය කරන කලාපය තුළ ශ්‍රී ලංකාවේ
කථාව තරම්‌ වේගවන්‌ යළි පිබිදීම පිළිබඳ කථාවක්‌ තවත්‌ ඇත්තනේ
නැහැ කීයලා. මූලාසනාරූඞ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනී, මේවා හිතලු කියලා
කවුරු හරි කියනවා නම්‌, මේවා ජයග්‍රහණ නොවෙයි කියලා කවුරු
භරි කීයනවා නම්‌, පැහැදිලිවම ඒවා කුහක, වෛරී ප්‍රකාශ
හැටියටයි අපි දකින්නේ. ඒ කියන්නේ ඒ අයට මේ ජයග්‍රහණයට,
මේ මල්‌ චට්ටියට අත ගහන්න බැරිවීම මත කරන ප්‍රකාශ
හැටියටයි අපි එම ප්‍රකාශ දකින්නේ, මූලාසනාරූස්‌ ගරු
මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි.

2024 අවුරුද්ද තුළ රාජ්‍ය සේවකයන්ට රුපියල්‌ 10,000ක
දීමනාවක්‌ ලබා දෙන්න අපට පුළුවන්කම ලැබී තිබෙනවා. ඒ
වෙලාවේ මේ රට තුළ විශාල වර්ජන රැල්ලක්‌ තිබුණා.
මූලාසනාරූඞ්‌ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමනි, හිටපු කෘෂිකර්ම ඇමතිවරයෙකු
චන අනුර කුමාර දිසානායක මහතනා, ගිටපු ඇමතිවරයෙකු වන
ලාල්කාන්ත මහතා ඇතුළු ජනතා විමුක්ති පෙරමුණේ
සාමාජිකයන්‌ එම චර්ජන රැල්ල ක්‍රියාත්මක කරද්දී අපේ රටේ
ජනතාව ඒ වර්ජන රැල්ලට ඉදිරියෙන්‌ සිටියේ. එදා දුම්රිය
සේවකයන්‌ ස්ට්‍රයික්‌ කරද්දී අපේ රටේ ගෞරවනීය ජනතාව අපට

ගරු ජයන්න සමරවීර මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு ஜயந்த சமரவீர)

(The Hon. Jayantha Samaraweera)

මූලාසනාරූඞ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමීයනි, අපරාධ නඩු විධාන සංග්‍රහය
(සංශෝධන) පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතන්‌, විදේශ නඩු තීන්දු අනෝ‍යෝනාව
පිළිගැනීම, ලියාපදිංචි කිරීම සහ බලාත්මක කිරීම පිළිබඳ පනන්‌
කෙටුම්පතත්‌, සේවකයන්ගේ ජාතික අවම වේතනය (සංශෝධන)
පනත්‌ කෙටුම්පතත්‌ සාකච්ඡාවට භාජන චන මේ වෙලාවේ ඒ
පිළිබඳව විපක්ෂයේ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමන්ලා දරපු අදහස්වලට
මුළුමනින්ම මාගේ එකහතාව පළ කරමින්‌, විශේෂයෙන්‌ අපරාධ
නඩු විධාන සංග්‍රහයට අදාළ කාරණයට පාර්ශ්වීයව බලපාන
කරුණක්‌ පිළිබඳව, මේ සමාජයේ, මේ ගරු සභාවේ හරිහමන්‌
අවධානයකට ලක්‌ නොවුණු, බැරෑරුම්‌ ප්‍රහාරයක්‌ පිළිබඳව මේ ගරු
සභාවේ අවධානය යොමු කරවලා, ජාතික උරුමයන්‌ සුරැකීම
උදෙසා ක්‍රියාත්මක වීම පිණිස වන පාර්ලිමේන්තු මන්ත්‍රී සංසදය
මඟින්‌ පත්කරන ලද අනුකමිටුව විසින්‌ සකස්‌ කරන ලද. බුදු දහම්‌
භා ඉතිහාසය විකෘති කිරීම වැළැක්වීම සඳහා නිර්දේශ ඉදිරිපත්‌
කිරීම පිළිබඳ චාර්තාව සභාගත කරන්න මම බලාපොරොත්තු
වෙනවා.

එය ආගමික කටයුතු හා සහජීවනය පිළිබඳ ආංශික
අධීක්ෂණ කාරක සභාවටත්‌, බුද්ධශාසන, ආගමික සහ
සංස්කෘතික කටයුතු පිළිබඳ අමාත්‍යාංශයිය උපදේශක කාරක
සභාවටන්‌ යොමු කරන ලෙස ඔබතුමියගෙන්‌ ඉල්ලා සිටිනවා.

මූලාසනාරූස්‌ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමියනි, අපි ඉන්නේ අපේ
ඉතිහාසයේ ඉතාම අවිනිශ්චිත මොහොතක කියලා කිව්වොත්‌ මම
ஐஐ මම වඩා නිවැරදියි කියලා. වෙන්නේ කුමක්ද කියලා, විය
හැක්කේ කුමක්ද කියලා කිසිදු නිශ්චිතතාවක්‌, කිසිදු ස්ථිරතාවක්‌
නොමැති මොහොතකයි අපි ඉන්නේ. අපි වැටී තිබෙන මේ
ශෞචනීය ආර්ථික තත්ත්වයෙන්‌, ඛේදනීය තත්ත්වයෙන්‌ ගොඩ
ඒම "චැල්‌ පාලමෙන්‌ එගොඩවීම හැර අන්කිසිවක්‌ නොවෙයි"
කියලා එකා පරයා එකා කියමින්‌ ඉන්න චේලාවකයි අපි ඉන්නේ.
අපි නම්‌ විශ්වාස කරන්නේ නැහැ, "දැන්‌ ඉතින්‌ කරන්න දෙයක්‌
නැහැ, වැල්‌ පාලමෙන්‌ එගොඩ වෙලා යන්න ඕනෑ ඉතුරු ටිකත්‌"
කියලා, මේ අප වැටී තිබෙන බිහිසුණු ආර්ථික අර්බුදයෙන්‌, මේ
ශෞචනීයභාවයෙන්‌, බංකොලොතනත්භාවයෙන්‌ අපට ගොඩ එන්න
පුළුවන්‌ වෙයි කියලා. ඒ නිසා තමයි "සර්වජන බලය" දේශපාලන
සන්ධානය හැටියට අපි මේ ජනාධිපතිවරණයට ඇවිල්ලා, "එක්ව

නංවන රටක්‌ - සතුට පිරුණු දැයක්‌" හැටියට මේ රට
ගොඩනගන්නේ කොහොමද කීයලා සර්වජන අපේක්ෂකයා

සළඳහා අපට සහයෝගය දැක්වූ කථානායක ගරු මගින්ද යාපා
අබේවර්ධන මැතිතුමාටත්‌, පාර්ලිමේන්තුවේ මහ ලේකම්‌ කුෂානි
රෝහණදීර මැතිතුමියටත්‌, කාරක සභා කාර්යාංශයේ සියලු
නිලධාරීන්ටත්‌ අපේ කෘතවේද්‍රිභාවය පළ කරමින්‌, එකී මන්ත්‍රී
සංසදය සකස්‌ කළ මෙම චාර්තාව ක්‍රියාවට නහන්න කියා ඉතා
ඕනෑකමින්‌ ඉල්ලා සිටිමින්‌, මගේ කථාව අවසන්‌ කරනවා,
මූලාසනාරූඞ ගරු මන්ත්‍රීතුමීයනි.

லர்‌ இழு මන්ත්‍රීතුමිය

(மாண்புமிகு தலைமைதாங்கும்‌ உறுப்பினர்‌ அவர்கள்‌)

(The Hon. Presiding Member)

ගරු වී. රාධාක්‍රිෂ්ණන්‌ මැතිතුමා. ඔබතුමාට විනාඩි 9ක
කාලයක්‌ තිබෙනවා.

727 2024 සැප්තැම්බර්‌ 03 728

[பி.ப. 3.36]

ගරු (ආචාර්ය) වී. රාධාක්‍රිෂ්ණන්‌ මහතා

(மாண்புமிகு (கலாநிதி) வீ. இராதாகிருஷ்ணன்‌)

(The Hon. (Dr.) V. Radhakrishnan)

கெளரவ தலைமைதாங்கும்‌ உறுப்பினர்‌ அவர்களே,
இலங்கையிலே வேலையாளர்களின்‌ ஆகக்குறைந்த வேதனம்‌
பற்றித்‌ தீர்மானிக்கின்ற திருத்தச்‌ சட்டமூலம்‌ இங்கு விவாதத்‌
துக்காக முன்வைக்கப்பட்டிருக்கின்றது. கடந்த காலங்களிலே
ஆகக்குறைந்த மாதாந்தச்‌ சம்பளமாக இருந்த 12,500 ரூபாய்‌
இதன்மூலம்‌ 17,500 ரூபாயாக உயர்த்தப்படவிருக்கின்றது.
அதன்படி ஒரு நாளுக்கு 500 ரூபாய்‌ என்றிருந்தது இப்பொழுது
700 ரூபாயாக மாற்றப்பட்டிருக்கின்றது. இந்தச்‌ சொச்ச
சம்பளத்தின்‌ மூலமாக இன்று வாழ முடியாது என்று நாங்கள்‌
தெரிந்துகொண்டாலும்‌ அரசாங்கத்தின்‌ ஆகக்குறைந்த சம்பளம்‌
என்ற அடிப்படையிலே இது முன்மொழியப்பட்டிருக்கின்றது.

அதேநேரத்தில்‌, தொழிலாளர்களின்‌

சம்பளப்‌ பிரச்சினை இன்று பூதாகரமானதாக மாறியிருக்கின்‌

பெருந்தோட்டத்‌

றது. பெருந்தோட்ட மக்களுடைய நாட்‌ சம்பளம்‌ 1,700 ரூபாய்‌
பிறகு 1,300 ரூபாய்‌
சொல்லப்பட்டது. ஆனால்‌, இந்த 1,300 ரூபாயும்‌ கிடைக்காத
நிலையில்‌ பிறகு மீண்டும்‌ 1,700 ரூபாய்‌ என்று சொல்லப்படு
கின்றது. எதுவுமே ஒரு கேள்விக்குறியான திலையில்தான்‌

என்று சொல்லப்பட்டது. என்று

காணப்படுகின்றது. அந்த வகையிலே, கடந்த 2 நாட்களுக்கு
முன்பு இங்கிருக்கின்ற எங்களுடைய பாராளுமன்ற உறுப்பினர்‌
எஸ்‌.பி. அவர்களும்‌, இப்பொழுது புதிதாக
நியமிக்கப்பட்ட இராஜாங்க அமைச்சர்‌ வடிவேல்‌ சுரேஷ்‌ அவர்‌
களும்‌ பேசிக்கொண்ட ஒரு சம்பாஷணையின்‌ அடிப்படை
கருத்துகள்‌ சமூக
பரவலாக வெளியிடப்பட்டுள்ளன. அதிலே “1,300 ரூபாய்‌

திசாநாயக்க

யிலான அவர்களுடைய ஊடகங்களில்‌
சம்பளத்தை எதிர்வரும்‌ 21ஆம்‌ திகதிக்கு முன்னர்‌ கொடுக்க
முடியுமா? அதற்காக ஏன்‌
என்றெல்லாம்‌ அவர்களால்‌ பேசப்பட்டிருக்கின்றது. அந்த

முயற்சி செய்யக்கூடாது?”

உரையாடலின்‌ இறுதியிலே, எஸ்‌.பி. திசாநாயக்க அவர்கள்‌
சொல்லுகின்றார்‌, “அவர்கள்‌ இந்தச்‌ சம்பளத்தைக்‌ கொடுக்கா
விட்டால்‌ அவர்களின்‌ வீடுகளுக்கு நெருப்பு வையுங்கள்‌!"
என்று. இது எவ்வளவு மோசமான வார்த்தைப்‌ பிரயோகம்‌
என்பதை நீங்கள்‌ தெரிந்துகொள்ள வேண்டும்‌. சம்பளம்‌
கொடுக்காவிட்டால்‌ அவர்களுடைய வீடுகளைத்‌ தீக்கிரை
யாக்க வேண்டுமென்று இப்படியான ஒரு நபர்‌ சொல்லுவது
மிகவும்‌ மோசமான, கண்டிக்கத்தக்க, அவமானமான ஒரு
செயல்‌ என்பதை நான்‌ இந்த நேரத்திலே சுட்டிக்காட்ட
விரும்புகின்றேன்‌.

அதேபோல பெருந்தோட்ட மக்களுடைய பிரச்சினைக்காக
முதலைக்‌ கண்ணீர்‌ வடித்து அதனைத்‌ தீர்ப்பதாகச்‌ சொன்ன
ஜனாதிபதி அவர்களும்‌ இன்று அதைப்பற்றி அசட்டையாக
அல்லது அக்கறையில்லாமல்‌ இருக்கின்றார்‌. ஆகவே, அவர்‌
களுடைய அதிகரிக்கப்பட்ட சம்பளம்‌ எதிர்வருகின்ற மாதத்‌
திலே கிடைக்காது என்பது இப்பொழுது உறுதியாகியிருக்‌
கின்றது. ஆனால்‌, எதிர்வரும்‌ காலங்களிலாவது அது அவர்‌
களுக்குக்‌ கிடைப்பதற்கான வழிகளைச்‌ சம்பந்தப்பட்டவர்கள்‌
செய்ய வேண்டும்‌ என்பதை இந்த சபையிலே கேட்டுக்கொள்ள

விரும்புகின்றேன்‌.

அதுமட்டுமல்லாமல்‌, இப்பொழுது சம்பள அதிகரிப்பு
இல்லையென்று சொல்லுகின்ற அதேவேளையிலே, தோட்டப்‌
பகுதிகளிலே அதிகமான 08% திறக்கப்படுவதை நாங்கள்‌
அவதானிக்கக்கூடியதாக இருக்கின்றது. நேற்று முன்தினம்‌
கூட ஹட்டன்‌ பிரதேசத்தில்‌ உள்ள குயில்வத்தை என்ற

பகுதியில்‌ 08 ஒன்றைத்‌ திறப்பதற்கான நடவடிக்கை எடுக்கப்‌

பட்டது; நாங்கள்‌ போய்‌ போராட்டம்‌ செய்து அதை
நிறுத்தியிருக்கின்றோம்‌. இன்று மக்கள்‌ வாழ்வாதாரம்‌
இல்லாமல்‌, சம்பளம்‌ இல்லாமல்‌ கஷ்டமான நிலையிலே

இருக்கின்றபோது, அவர்களிடம்‌ இருக்கின்ற பணத்தையும்‌
குடிக்காகச்‌ செலவழிக்கச்‌ செய்ய வேண்டுமென்று செயற்படு
கிறார்கள்‌. அண்மையிலே நான்‌ ஒரு வீடியோ பார்த்தேன்‌.
அதில்‌ ஜனாதிபதி அவர்கள்‌ சொல்லுகின்றார்‌, “08 திறந்தால்‌
என்ன தப்பு? அது இந்த நாட்டின்‌ வர்த்தகத்தை அதிகரிக்கும்‌”
என்று. இப்படியெல்லாம்‌ bars திறந்து வர்த்தகத்தை
அதிகரித்து, மக்களைத்‌ துன்பங்களுக்குள்ளாக்கித்‌ தாங்கள்‌
இந்த நாட்டினுடைய ஜனாதிபதியாக வரவேண்டும்‌ என்ற
எண்ணம்‌ அவர்களுக்கு இருந்தால்‌ அதை மாற்றிக்கொள்ள

வேண்டும்‌ என்பதை நான்‌ இங்கு சொல்லிக்கொள்ள
விரும்புகின்றேன்‌.

அதைவிட, இப்பொழுது பேசப்படுகின்ற ஒரு மிக
முக்கியமான விடயமாக இருப்பது மாகாண சபைகள்‌
பற்றியதாகும்‌. அரசியலமைப்பின்‌ 13ஆவது திருத்தத்தின்‌
அடிப்படையிலே மாகாண சபைகள்‌ உருவாக்கப்பட

வேண்டும்‌. வடக்கு, கிழக்கிற்கு மட்டும்‌ அல்ல, இலங்கையில்‌
இருக்கின்ற சகல பகுதிகளுக்கும்‌ மாகாண சபைகள்‌ தேவை
என்பதை நாங்கள்‌ அறிந்திருக்கின்றோம்‌. அந்த அடிப்படை
யில்‌, மாகாண சயைத்‌ தேர்தல்‌ பற்றிய திருத்தச்‌ சட்டமூல
மொன்றை கெளரவ சுமந்திரன்‌ அவர்கள்‌ ஒரு தனியார்‌
கொண்டுவந்திருந்தார்‌. அதன்‌ முதலாம்‌,
இரண்டாம்‌ வாசிப்பு முடிவடைந்து இன்று அது மூன்றாம்‌
வாசிப்புக்கு எடுக்கப்படவிருந்த நிலையில்‌, அதை எடுக்க

சட்டமூலமாகக்‌

விடாது மறுத்திருக்கின்றார்கள்‌. இதற்குக்‌ காரணம்‌,
நேற்றுமுன்‌ தினம்‌ இலங்கை தமிழரசுக்‌ கட்சி - [ரக -
ஜனாதிபதி வேட்பாளர்‌ சஜித்‌ பிரேமதாஸ அவர்களை
ஆதரிப்பதாகச்‌ சொன்னமையே ஆகும்‌. அதன்‌

காரணமாகத்தான்‌ தமிழ்‌ மக்க ளுக்கு மாகாண சபைக்கான

உரிமையைக்‌ கொடுக்கக்கூடாது, அதனை இல்லாமல்‌
ஆக்கவேண்டுமென்ற அடிப்படையிலே இந்தச்‌ சட்டமூலம்‌
தட்டிக்கழிக்கப்பட்டிருப்பதாக நாங்கள்‌ காண்கின்றோம்‌. இனத்‌
துவேசத்தை இங்கு
முறைமையை இல்லாமல்‌ செய்வது தமிழர்களுக்கு மட்டுமல்ல,

கொண்டுவந்து மாகாண சபை
இந்த நாட்டில்‌ வாழுகின்ற முஸ்லிம்‌ மக்களுக்கும்‌ சிங்கள
மக்களுக்கும்‌ பாதிப்பை ஏற்படுத்தும்‌. ஏனென்றால்‌, மாகாண
சபை முறைமை என்பது வடக்கு, கிழக்குக்கு மட்டும்‌
உரித்தானதல்ல. ஒன்பது மாகாணங்‌ களுக்கும்‌ இந்தச்‌ சபை
மூலமாக வேலைகள்‌ மேற்கொள்ள வேண்டிய கட்டாயம்‌
இருக்கின்றது. இந்தச்‌ சட்டமூலத்தை தமிழரான கெளரவ
சுமந்திரன்‌ அவர்கள்‌ கொண்டுவந்தார்‌ என்பதற்காகத்‌
தடுத்தார்களா? என்ற சந்தேகம்கூட இப்‌ பொழுது எங்களுக்கு
எழுகின்றது. இந்த நிலை மாற்றமடைய வேண்டுமென்று
நாங்கள்‌ சொல்லிக்கொள்கின்றோம்‌.

இப்பொழுது ஜனாதிபதி தேர்தல்‌ பிரசாரங்கள்‌ இடம்‌
பெற்றுக்‌ கொண்டு இருக்கின்றன. 2015இலே ஜனாதிபதித்‌
தேர்தலின்போது “66 5” என்று பிரசாரம்‌ செய்தார்கள்‌;
2019இலே “ஸ்கிம ஈஐஐ௧6” என்று பிரசாரம்‌ செய்தார்கள்‌.
இப்பொழுது 2024இலே “௦;8ீ சஜ
செய்கிறார்கள்‌. ஒவ்வொரு ஜனாதிபதித்‌ தேர்தலின்போதும்‌
இவ்வாறான  'ஈஐ௦௦3 வந்துகொண்டுதான்‌ இருக்கின்றது.
தேர்தல்கள்‌ வரும்போது இவ்வாறான விடயங்களைச்‌ சொல்லி
குழப்பி,

729 පාර්ලිමේන්තුව 730

[ගරු (පාචාර්ය) වී. රාධාක්‍රිෂ්ණන්‌ මහතා]

யொன்று கேள்விப்படுகிறோம்‌. அதாவது, யார்‌ ஜனாதிபதி
யாக வந்தாலும்‌, ஆறு மாதங்களின்‌ பின்னர்‌ திரும்பவும்‌
மாண்புமிகு ரணில்‌ விக்கிரமசிங்ஹ அவர்கள்தான்‌ நாட்டின்‌
ஜனாதிபதியாக வரப்போகின்றாரென்று. இது எப்படி
உறுதியாகும்‌? நான்‌ சொல்கின்றேன்‌, இந்த ஜனாதிபதி நூறு
வருடங்கள்‌ வாழ வேண்டும்‌; அதில்‌ எந்தவிதமான ஆட்சேப
னையும்‌ கிடையாது. ஆனால்‌, இந்த ஜனாதிபதிக்கு ஏதாவது
ஏற்பட்டால்‌, இந்த நாட்டை விற்கப்போகிறீர்களா அல்லது
வெளிநாட்டிலிருந்து ஒருவரைக்‌ கொண்டுவந்து இங்கு
ஜனாதிபதி ஆக்கப்போகிறீர்களா?

මේ ජනාධිපතිතුමා අවුරුදු 100ක්‌, 200ක්‌ මේ රටේ ඉන්න

6කින්‌ තව ජනාධිපති කෙනෙක්‌ එනවා කියලා. චාමර සම්පත්‌
රාජ්‍ය ඇමතිතුමා ජනාධිපතිතුමාට කියලා තිබෙනවා ලු, "එහෙම්‌

ஆகவே, முதலைக்‌ கண்ணீர்‌ வடிக்கத்‌ தேவையில்லை.
எனக்கு ஒதுக்கப்பட்ட நேரம்‌ முடிவடைந்தமையால்‌ நான்‌
அதிகம்‌ பேச விரும்பவில்லை. இந்த நாட்டினுடைய நலனை
நோக்கி, மக்கள்‌ செல்வாக்குள்ள சஜித்‌ பிரேமதாஸ அவர்கள்‌
இந்த நாட்டினுடைய ஜனாதிபதியாக
எதிர்பார்ப்பு எங்களுக்கு இருக்கின்றது என்று கூறி, நிறைவு
செய்கின்றேன்‌. நன்றி.

ආයේ ප්‍රජාතන්ත්‍රවාදයක්‌ නැහැ, ඕනෑ මිනිහෙක්‌, ඕනෑ දේශපාලන
පක්ෂයක්‌ තහනම්‌ කරන්න, ඕනෑම විපක්ෂ නායකයෙක්‌,
වීරුද්ධවාදියෙක්‌ අන්‌අඩංගුවට ගන්න, ඕනෑ නම්‌ මරලා දාන්න,
රටින්‌ එළවන්න කරන මනවාදය සමාජයීය වශයෙන්‌ නහවුරු
කිරීම තමයි මේ කරන්නේ. අන්න ඒ භයානක සමාජ බෙදුම්වාදය
දීර්ඝ කාලීන කල්‌ අල්ලන මනවාදයක්‌. ඒ ගොල්ලන්ටත්‌ ඒක
(01:1110] කර ගන්න බැරි වෙනවා. එම්‌ නිසා මෙන්න මේක ගැන
ආර්ථික කාරණයටත්‌ වඩා අපි උනන්දු විය යුතුයි කියලා මම
මතක්‌ කරනවා. අද මේ රටට අවශ්‍ය වෙලා තිබෙන්නේ ඒ වාගේ
භයානක, ප්‍රචණ්ඩත්වයට අත වනන, ප්‍රායෝගීකත්වයට කිසි
ඉඩක්‌ නැති දේශපාලනයක්‌ නොවෙයි.

ගරු නියෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුමනි, මේ ජනාධිපතිවරණයෙන්‌
මේ රටේ ජනතාවට ඉස්පාසුවක්‌ අවශ්‍ය චෙලා තිබෙනවා. මේ
රටට හුස්ම ගන්න අවකාශයක්‌ අවශ්‍ය වෙලා තිබෙනවා. රට
කියන්නේ මිනිස්සු කියලා ගීතන නායකයෙකු යටතේ
මෙහෙයවන ප්‍රජාතන්ත්‍රවාදී රාජ්‍යයක්‌ අවශ්‍ය වෙලා තිබෙනවා.
අන්න ඒක නිසා ඔය සමාජ මාධ්‍ය අවකාශයේ, මාධ්‍ය අවකාශයේ,
6208 මහාචාර්යවරු කියන කචී නොවෙයි, මේ ගැන ඇහට
දැනෙන මිනිස්සු දසදහස්‌ ගණනක්‌ අද වන විට සමගී ජන
බලවේගය වටා ඒක රාශි වෙමින්‌ සිටිනවා. එම්‌ නීසා අපේ රටේ
අනාගතය අඳුරු නැහැ කීයන එකසි මම කියන්නේ. රට අඳුරට
ගෙන යන්න මොන අය උත්සාහ ගත්තන්‌ මේ රට ඉදිරියේ ලොකු
ආලෝකයක්‌ මතුවෙමින්‌ තිබෙනවාය කියන එක මතක්‌ කරමින්‌
මේ පාර්ලීමේන්තුවේ මගේ ප්‍රථම කථාව මෙතෙකින්‌ අවසන්‌
කරනවා.
